This is new, and it is the closest thing to a public statement of her own evolving relationship with lethal force she has ever offered. A surveillance-level read: the module exists because she is teaching herself.

Two students bear specific watch:
- A senior student, several years in, being slowly groomed as dōjō second — given keys, given the right to lock up, given the password to the intake voicemail. Colleen has not told her she is the next custodian of the Book.
- A newer student, eighteen months in, on whom Colleen has spent disproportionate time. The student's intake profile (trafficked, escaped, no family) maps onto Colleen's own *Marvel Premiere* #20 history with uncomfortable precision. The countertransference is visible to no one but Misty, who has not raised it.

## IV.g — Daily Pattern, Current

A surveillance-grade reconstruction of a representative current day:

- **0445** — wakes, no alarm, has not used an alarm in twenty years. Water, not coffee.
- **0500–0545** — solo practice on the dōjō floor below the loft. *Iaidō* draws, kata cycle (currently working through a Musō Shinden-ryū sequence she learned from her grandfather, plus two katas she composed herself in her thirties and has never named). Sword maintenance follows: *uchiko*, oil, cloth, inspection. The blade is cleaned whether or not it was drawn against anyone the prior day.
- **0545–0630** — seated meditation, kamidana facing east, then a light meal (rice, pickled vegetable, fish or egg, green tea).
- **0630–0730** — administrative window. Email (terse, often one-word replies), Daughters intake review with Misty by phone, dōjō scheduling.
- **0730–1200** — student instruction, individual sessions, scheduled in 50-minute blocks with 10-minute resets.
- **1200–1300** — second meal, often alone, occasionally with a student she is specifically observing. Reads — currently rereading her father's published work on Tang-era statecraft, an act she would not characterize as grief but which is.
- **1300–1700** — variable. Operations support, range day if scheduled, safehouse rotation check-ins, occasional consult on a Daughters case, occasional Rand-business signing.
- **1700–1900** — evening student block, group class, fewer individuals, more conditioning.
- **1900–2100** — second meditation, light reading, sword on the rack, lights low. If Misty calls, she answers. If Danny is in town, this window dissolves and she does not pretend otherwise.
- **2100–2130** — sleep, deep, six hours minimum, undisturbed unless phone rings on the short list (Misty, Danny, the senior student, two operational contacts).

Variations are minimal. The pattern has held with this rough shape for over a decade, with the only structural change being the gradual reduction of operational hours and the gradual expansion of instructional hours.

## IV.h — Somatic and Behavioral Tells, Current

- The **scar inventory** has stabilized; no significant new wounds in the latest period. The oldest scars — the forearm parry scars, a thigh scar she does not discuss that dates to a Kara-Kai-period operation, a small mark at the base of the throat from the trafficking attempt — she does not hide and does not display.
- Her **left wrist** has begun to grumble in cold weather; she has modified her grip and adjusted certain kata to compensate, and she has not consulted a physician. She has consulted, instead, an acupuncturist Misty referred her to, monthly, in Chinatown.
- The **resettling-the-saya** tell remains diagnostic. When she goes still and her left thumb finds the *koiguchi*, the situation has been assessed and the decision has been made. This is unchanged from her thirties.
- A **newer tell**, present only in the last several years: in conversations she finds difficult, she will lift her tea (or whatever is at hand) and hold it, not drink it, for several beats longer than the conversation requires. The cup is a containment object. The longer it is held without drinking, the more material is being held back.
- **Sleep posture**: right side, blade within reach but not within the bed. This has not changed in forty years and will not.

## IV.i — Current Threat Posture

She is, at present, **not actively hunted** by any specific organization. The Kara-Kai is functionally collapsed; Emil Vachon's network is generations dispersed; the Hand has bigger problems than her. Her threat exposure is now primarily **incidental** — operations she takes on for the Daughters that put her in proximity to traffickers, predator networks, and the lower tiers of organized crime, none of which know her by name and most of which learn it once.

Her **counter-surveillance posture** is competent but unfussy. She varies routes; she clocks tails; she sweeps the dōjō quarterly with a contractor Misty trusts. She does not use signal-grade tradecraft because she does not believe she is interesting enough at the federal level to warrant it, which is, from a Watcher-grade perspective, *almost correct*. She is interesting at the federal level chiefly through her proximity to Rand and to the broader street-hero ecosystem, and the relevant agencies treat her as a peripheral node — observed, catalogued, not pursued.

## IV.j — Internal State, Best Available Reconstruction

She is, in the present period, the most settled she has ever been, and the most quietly braced. The settledness is real: the dōjō works, the partnership with Misty works, the institutional role suits her, the students give her a generative outlet she did not know she required. She is, at sixty-plus published years and whatever in-universe age the current canon assigns, *good at her life* in a way she was not at twenty-five or forty.

The bracing is for the loss she has not yet metabolized and is preparing for at the level of paperwork: Danny, eventually and permanently. And, beneath that, the older bracing she has carried since the trafficking attempt and the Kara-Kai conditioning, which is the steady low-grade vigilance of someone who has had her body taken three times and has organized her entire adult life around not letting it happen a fourth.

The warrior-monk presentation holds. The containers are intact. The discipline is sharp. The cup is held for slightly longer than the conversation requires.

She is, at present, exactly who she has spent fifty years becoming. The question the file leaves open — the one she does not ask herself and no one asks her — is what she becomes if one of the containers gives way.


## Medical History

# MEDICAL HISTORY — COLLEEN WING

*UATU Dossier, Section 2 of 12. Compiled from longitudinal canon record (1974–present), cross-referenced against operational sightings, sparring footage, dōjō intake forms recovered from Nightwing Restorations and the West 50th Street school, and field-medic notes from Rand Enterprises' private clinic on East 72nd. Subject has no NHS, VA, or major-insurer file; primary medical relationship is with a Dr. Sasaki (internist, Murray Hill, Japanese-American Medical Society referral, seen approximately annually) and with an unlicensed Chinatown bonesetter on Doyers Street used for acute musculoskeletal work. No psychiatric record exists in any jurisdiction.*

---

## 2.1 CONSTITUTIONAL BASELINE

Subject presents as a peak-conditioned human female, mid-to-late biological age depending on sliding chronology, of mixed Japanese–European ancestry. Height approximately 5'6"; weight cycles within a narrow 125–135 lb band tied to training intensity rather than dietary fluctuation. Resting heart rate, based on observed neck pulse in static surveillance footage, is in the high 40s — a marker of decades of sustained aerobic and breath-discipline work (zazen, *Mokusō* before kata). Blood pressure normotensive. Body fat is low but not depleted; she carries enough subcutaneous reserve to indicate she has not adopted the chronic underfeeding pattern common to some martial purists — her grandfather's instruction evidently included a Japanese country-kitchen relationship to food (rice, fish, pickled vegetables, miso) that she has maintained into adulthood, augmented in New York by a tolerant omnivory.

No known metahuman factor, mutant gene, mystical empowerment, or surgical/cybernetic augmentation. She is, in the literal medical sense, a baseline human — which, given her operational performance against superhuman opposition, is itself a clinical datum. The body she fields is the body she trained.

Blood type: O-positive (donor card on file with the Greater New York Blood Program, last donation logged ~14 months ago — a habit, not a one-off; she gives quarterly when her wound calendar permits).

---

## 2.2 DEVELOPMENTAL AND CHILDHOOD MEDICAL

Born in Japan to Azumi Ozawa and Professor Lee Wing. Maternal death occurred in subject's early childhood; cause not specified in any obtainable record, but the temporal proximity to subject's relocation to her grandfather's mountain household suggests an illness severe enough to displace primary caregiving rather than an acute accident. Subject has never spoken publicly of her mother's medical end; the absence is itself information.

Childhood and adolescence on Honshu under Kenji Ozawa's roof produced the foundational musculoskeletal architecture: skeletal loading from daily kata beginning before epiphyseal closure has given her the characteristic adult swordsman's frame — slightly elevated bone density in the right radius and ulna, mature rotator cuff development bilaterally with right-side dominance, and an unusually deep transverse abdominis recruitment pattern visible when she breathes. Childhood diet was traditional and adequate; no rickets, no early dental caries (she has a full set of natural teeth, lightly worn at the molars from sleep-bruxism — see §2.6). Mountain altitude and clean air mean her pulmonary baseline is excellent; no childhood asthma, no scarring on imaging.

Menarche presumed normative; menstrual cycle reportedly regular until the operational decades, when intensity of training and episodic blood loss from wounds have produced occasional secondary amenorrhea of 1–3 months' duration — a pattern she manages without intervention.

No childhood surgeries. No vaccinations record outside the Japanese standard schedule. Subject was an unusually healthy child of the kind that disciplined rural Japanese pediatric care tended to produce: few infections, none serious, and a learned stoicism around minor injury that her grandfather reinforced rather than soothed.

---

## 2.3 THE NEW YORK RUPTURE — FIRST TOXICOLOGICAL EVENT (1974)

Arrival in Manhattan in late adolescence/early adulthood to live with Professor Wing. Within weeks, the Vachon abduction. She was overpowered on the street, injected with a sedative compound (the period record is imprecise; consistent with a barbiturate or short-acting benzodiazepine, possibly cut with an opioid for compliance — the trafficking network's chemistry was crude), and held for transport. Rescue by Daniel Rand and Misty Knight occurred before she was moved out of city; she emerged with the puncture site healed in days but with the somatic memory durable.

**Medical sequelae:**
- Acute: 36–48 hours of post-sedation grogginess, ataxia, and (per Misty Knight's later off-hand reference) significant vomiting. No long-term hepatic or renal injury on subsequent panels.
- Chronic: subject thereafter declines all systemic anesthesia except under conditions she controls. She has refused IV sedation for at least two documented surgical events (see §2.5), opting for local infiltration and conscious endurance — a preference her surgeons have learned not to argue.
- Behavioral: she does not drink from glasses she has not poured or watched poured. She does not accept open beverages in clubs, at parties, or from strangers. In her own apartment she keeps a kettle and a sealed sake supply. In Misty's apartment she will drink from anything Misty hands her; the trust is total and unique.

This is the first instance — and the founding template — of what becomes the dominant theme of her medical file: **involuntary loss of bodily sovereignty**, and the precise, narrow, lifelong behavioral compensations that follow.

---

## 2.4 CUMULATIVE OCCUPATIONAL WEAR — THE SWORDSMAN'S SIGNATURE

Twenty-plus years of daily *iaidō*, *kenjutsu*, jūjutsu cross-training, and live operational use of a *katana* and *wakizashi* have left a predictable, granular musculoskeletal signature. A skilled sports-medicine physician examining her cold would derive most of her professional history from her body alone.

**Hands.** Calluses at the base of the right index and middle fingers, second knuckles, and the heel of both palms — the characteristic *tsuka*-grip pattern. The right thumb pad is thickened; the left, slightly less so. Fingernails are kept short and squared, no polish, ever. A thin scar runs across the web of the left thumb from a poorly-controlled *nukitsuke* draw in adolescence — her grandfather, per family report, did not bandage it for her.

**Forearms.** Hypertrophied flexor and extensor compartments bilaterally. Visible vascularity even at rest. Multiple thin transverse scars on the anterior left forearm (3–5 distinct, the longest approximately 11 cm, running from mid-forearm toward the wrist) — the parrying record. The right forearm is cleaner; she cuts more than she blocks on that side. There is a single deeper diagonal scar on the right dorsal forearm from a Hand *ninjatō* during the Master Khan period (see §2.7) that required field suturing and healed with mild keloid.

**Shoulders.** Right rotator cuff shows chronic micro-tear pattern — supraspinatus tendinopathy, well-managed, never surgically addressed. She self-treats with an unmarked Tiger Balm analog from a Mott Street herbalist and with a specific shoulder-mobility kata she runs on waking. Left shoulder is markedly cleaner. There is a healed posterior dislocation on the right (estimated date: late Power Man and Iron Fist period) reduced in the field by Misty Knight using a leverage technique Misty learned in NYPD ESU training — Colleen has spoken of it once, drily, as "the most painful favor she ever did me."

**Wrists.** Bilateral mild carpal tunnel symptoms (occasional nocturnal paresthesias in the right median nerve distribution) which she manages by sleeping with the wrist in neutral on a small buckwheat-husk pillow. No surgical decompression.

**Spine.** Lumbar wear consistent with thousands of rotational kata. L4–L5 disc space narrowed mildly on imaging. No radiculopathy. Thoracic mobility is exceptional for her age cohort — the breathing discipline preserves it. Cervical spine clean.

**Hips and knees.** Hips are mobile and symmetric. Right knee shows a small, asymptomatic effusion seasonally tied to floor-kneeling-heavy seiza weeks in the dōjō; she manages it with ice, elevation, and a stubborn refusal to modify the lesson plan. Patellar tendons thick bilaterally.

**Feet.** Splayed forefoot from decades of barefoot dōjō training. Callus pattern on the lateral edges from *suri-ashi* (sliding foot). One healed metatarsal stress fracture, right second ray, untreated at time of injury and unionized slightly malaligned — visible as a small bump she does not notice.

**Eyes.** Visual acuity uncorrected 20/15 right, 20/20 left. No glasses, no contacts. She reads small text in low light better than her father did at her age. She blinks notably less than population baseline — a sword-trained habit that surveillance-quality footage picks up immediately as a tell.

**Ears.** Hearing intact across frequencies. No tinnitus despite firearms exposure with Misty — she wears foam plugs at every range visit, a discipline imported from her grandfather's general respect for the senses.

**Skin.** A surveyor's map. Beyond the forearm scars: a longitudinal scar across the left lateral thigh from an edged weapon during the Daughters of the Dragon period (approximately 18 cm, well-healed, no contracture); a puncture scar in the right paraspinal at T9 from a shuriken in the Master Khan era; a gunshot entry-exit pair through the soft tissue of the left flank (no organ involvement, treated at Rand's private clinic, no laparotomy needed); a small crescent scar above the right eyebrow from a thrown bottle in the trafficking attempt; faded suture-line scars on the right lateral calf (8 cm) and the left supraclavicular fossa (4 cm, the latter alarmingly close to the subclavian and the one she touches absently when tired); two healed cigarette-burn scars on the inner left arm, small, paired, of unclear provenance — she has never explained them, and the placement suggests interrogation rather than self-harm. No tattoos. No piercings beyond a single set of small lobe holes she rarely uses.

She does not show these scars. She trains in long-sleeved gi even in summer, swims in private, and changes in stalls. This is not shame; it is curation. The body is an operational document and she does not publish it.

---

## 2.5 ACUTE TRAUMATIC EVENTS — SURGICAL AND FIELD-MEDICAL HISTORY

A non-exhaustive ledger of the documented major events:

- **Gunshot wound, left flank, through-and-through, soft tissue only.** Treated at Rand Enterprises' private clinic. Local anesthesia, irrigation, primary closure, oral antibiotics. Subject was ambulatory within 36 hours and resumed light kata at 96 hours against medical advice.
- **Edged-weapon laceration, left lateral thigh, ~18 cm, partial-thickness through the vastus lateralis fascia.** Field-pressure dressing by Misty Knight; definitive closure at a Chinatown clinic that does not log names. Subject walked with a barely perceptible left-leg compensation for approximately three weeks; the gait correction was complete and the limp does not recur under fatigue, which is unusually clean healing and speaks to her rehabilitation discipline.
- **Penetrating injury, right paraspinal T9, shuriken, depth ~3 cm, narrowly missing the pleura.** Removed in the field, packed, sutured later. The scar tissue produces an occasional muscular catch on deep right-rotation; she has incorporated a counter-stretch into morning kata.
- **Right shoulder posterior dislocation,** reduced in the field, no surgical stabilization. Subject has refused arthroscopic workup despite three separate medical recommendations across two decades.
- **Multiple rib contusions and at least two non-displaced rib fractures** (left 7th and right 9th, on separate occasions) from blunt impact during operations. Both managed conservatively. She breathes through it; the breath discipline is, by her account, the entire therapy.
- **Concussions:** at least three documented mild-to-moderate TBIs over career, including one with brief loss of consciousness during the Kara-Kai episode. No formal neurocognitive testing was ever done. Subjectively she reports occasional brief word-finding lapses in Japanese (not English) which she ascribes to disuse rather than injury — possibly correct, possibly not.
- **One full surgical event under local anesthesia only:** repair of a deep right-hand laceration that nicked a flexor tendon, performed by a hand surgeon at NYU who later said, on background, that he had never operated on a more still patient. She watched. She declined the sedative he offered three times.

There are no elective procedures in her record. No cosmetic work. No orthodontics. No LASIK. No fertility intervention. The body is what it is and she negotiates with it.

---

## 2.6 SLEEP, APPETITE, LIBIDO, MENSTRUAL

**Sleep.** Approximately 5.5–6.5 hours, biphasic when she can manage it (a long night sleep plus a 20-minute afternoon *inemuri* in seiza, a habit retained from her grandfather). Sleep onset is rapid — the breath discipline doubles as a sleep induction protocol. Mild nocturnal bruxism, evidenced by molar wear and an occasional jaw soreness she ignores. She sleeps on a futon on tatami in her own apartment; in field conditions she sleeps anywhere, in any posture, fully. She wakes once around 4 a.m. on most nights, briefly, alert, then returns to sleep — a pattern she has had since adolescence and which she interprets as normal. The 4 a.m. wake is the seam where dream material that has not been processed surfaces; she does not pursue it.

**Appetite.** Regular, modest, disciplined. Two main meals and a small breakfast. Strong preference for Japanese home-style cooking, with selective enthusiasms for Sichuan and for Misty's terrible coffee. She does not snack. She does not skip meals under stress — she eats *more* deliberately under stress, recognizing the operational cost of skipped fuel.

**Libido.** Normative on the available record. Sexual behavior is private, monogamous when partnered, and not a site of dysregulation. The romantic record with Daniel Rand reads as warm, intermittent, and ungrasping. There is no evidence of compulsive or avoidant sexual patterning. Whether the Vachon trauma left a specific sexual-assault-coded inhibition is undeterminable from outside; her behavior is consistent with a person who has integrated the event without erasure.

**Menstrual.** As noted, generally regular with occasional stress-induced or blood-loss-induced amenorrhea. Cramping reportedly mild. She trains through it.

---

## 2.7 INVOLUNTARY ALTERATIONS — THE THREE INVASIONS

This is the single most clinically important cluster in subject's file, and the one that her composure most successfully obscures.

### 2.7.1 The Trafficking Sedation (chronicled §2.3)

The founding event. A chemical override of consciousness in the service of another's plan to commodify her body. The behavioral footprint is permanent and detailed (the beverage rule, the sedation refusal, the curated unwillingness to be unconscious in a space she does not control).

### 2.7.2 The Kara-Kai Conditioning

Capture and programming by Master Khan's apparatus. The methodology, reconstructible from canonical fragments and from the standard practices of fictional conditioning operations of that era, combined hypnotic induction, sleep deprivation, sensory manipulation, and pharmacological adjuncts (likely a dissociative agent paired with a stimulant — the operational profile of someone running a conditioned subject requires both suggestibility and motor competence). She was deployed as an assassin against people she loved, and she nearly killed Misty Knight.

**Medical sequelae:**
- Acute, post-deconditioning: a period of disorientation, intermittent dissociative episodes (rare for her), and at least one documented panel of weeping — almost the only such instance in the canonical record. The weeping was alone, brief, and followed by an immediate return to operational composure.
- Subacute: weight loss of an estimated 8–12 lb over the following weeks; mild insomnia of approximately a month's duration; an intensification of kata practice (compensatory ritual loading).
- Chronic: she has never used a hypnotic or guided-meditation app, audio file, or practice that involves another voice instructing her into altered state. Her meditation is silent, self-directed, and her own. She is the only voice in her head when her eyes are closed. This is non-negotiable and unspoken.
- Chronic, relational: a slight, durable hesitation before drawing on Misty in sparring. A reluctance to spar Misty live-edge that did not exist before. Neither of them mentions it. Both of them know.

Moral-injury weight (per §4 of the workup) is the dominant frame here; the medical face of that injury is the chronic background hum of an unprocessed violation that she has chosen, with full awareness, to leave unprocessed because the processing tools available (talk therapy, group work, psychiatric medication) are not coded as honorable inside her operating system. The cost is real. The cost is also chosen.

### 2.7.3 The Vampiric Transformation

A late-Claremont-era transformation, reversed. For the duration she was something other than human: photophobic, blood-driven, with the altered metabolism and perceptual shifts that the condition entails. Reversal restored baseline.

**Medical sequelae:**
- No detectable hematologic residue; standard CBC unremarkable.
- A reportedly heightened photosensitivity for several months post-reversal — she wore sunglasses more, trained at dawn or dusk rather than midday, and avoided beach light.
- A specific dietary aversion to undercooked meat that persisted for years and may persist still — she orders steak well-done and fish thoroughly seared, a preference that reads as eccentric for someone of her culinary sophistication and is, in fact, a quiet trauma residue.
- A reluctance to be photographed with flash, which she frames as general dislike of cameras but which dates from this period.

Three invasions. Three different vectors — pharmacological, psychological-cum-pharmacological, and supernatural-biological. The body she fields has been overridden three documented times by three different mechanisms. A fourth such event would, in this analyst's assessment, represent the single greatest threat to her psychological integrity that her enemies could engineer — far greater than physical injury, capture, or even the death of a peer.

---

## 2.8 SUBSTANCES

- **Alcohol:** moderate. Sake in cultural and social contexts; the occasional beer with Misty; almost no spirits. No pattern of dependence. She has never been observed publicly intoxicated.
- **Tobacco:** none.
- **Cannabis:** none on record. The preference for unaltered cognition is structural.
- **Stimulants:** caffeine — green tea daily, sometimes hojicha in the evening (which she tolerates because she sleeps regardless). She tolerates Misty's filter coffee out of affection rather than taste.
- **Prescription medications:** none chronic. Occasional NSAIDs (ibuprofen) for acute musculoskeletal pain; she resists even these, preferring topical liniments and rest.
- **Performance-enhancing substances:** none. She would consider them a contamination of the discipline.
- **Recreational pharmacology:** none on record.

The substance profile is the substance profile of someone for whom altered states are coded as danger, not pleasure. The Vachon event is the etiology; the Kara-Kai event is the reinforcement.

---

## 2.9 PSYCHIATRIC MEDICAL RECORD

None. No diagnosis, no medication, no inpatient stay, no outpatient course, no documented contact with a mental health professional in any jurisdiction. Subject has never sought, nor been referred to, nor (to this analyst's knowledge) seriously considered psychiatric care. The cultural and personal coding of distress as a private somatic-ritual problem, not an interpersonal-verbal one, is total.

The clinical observation embedded in this absence: subject's containment apparatus (dōjō, sword, Misty, the Daughters of the Dragon institution, the daily kata) is doing the work that, in a different person, a psychiatric record would document. The apparatus is sufficient. The apparatus is also single-point-of-failure-prone. Were the dōjō destroyed, the sword lost, Misty killed, and the Daughters dispersed in a single operational window, this file would expect a decompensation event — most likely manifesting as a sharp, contained depressive episode with somatic features (sleep collapse, appetite loss, training cessation) followed by a slow, self-directed rebuild around a new container. She would not seek help. She would survive it. The survival would cost.

---

## 2.10 SUMMARY MEDICAL FORMULATION

A baseline-human female operator at the upper end of unaugmented physical performance, carrying the full musculoskeletal ledger of a lifetime sword discipline and the full scar ledger of two decades of frontline mercenary work, in a state of preserved general health maintained by exceptional ritual self-care and a near-total avoidance of the medical system. Three documented episodes of involuntary bodily alteration constitute the most psychologically loaded — and least clinically addressed — material in her file. Substance use minimal; sleep and appetite preserved; libido normative; affect regulation excellent and somatically achieved. No psychiatric record exists and none will exist absent a containment-system collapse her enemies have not yet engineered.

The body is the document. She has been editing it carefully for forty years.


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS: COLLEEN WING

*File subsection: bodily record, longitudinal observation. Cross-referenced against thirty-plus years of canon appearance and inferred from training lineage, occupational load, and documented bodily-invasion history. The body is the primary text; she leaves more in it than she will ever leave in speech.*

---

## I. STANDING ARCHITECTURE

**Baseline stance.** Feet at approximately shoulder width, weight distributed 55/45 onto the rear leg — a *hanmi*-derived ready-stance disguised as ordinary standing. The civilian eye reads it as good posture; a fellow swordsman reads it as a person who has not actually relaxed since adolescence. Knees never locked. Pelvis under-tucked perhaps half a degree forward of neutral, loading the hara. The center of gravity sits low and rearward, available for either retreat or commitment without weight-shift telegraph.

**Spine.** Lumbar slightly extended, thoracic open, cervical long — what kenjutsu instructors call "the string from crown to coccyx." Has trained this into involuntary geometry; even sleeping she does not curl tightly. Decades of *kata* repetition have built mild lumbar wear (likely L4–L5 facet load) that she manages through morning *shiko*-style hip openers, not analgesics.

**Hands at rest.** Right hand falls slightly forward of the right hip — the position the hand would occupy if a *katana* were worn at the obi. She is not conscious of this. The thumb of the right hand rests against the side of the index finger as if seated on a *tsuka*-end. When standing in conversation she will, perhaps every ninety seconds, briefly cup her left hand at her left hip in the *saya*-hand position before letting it drop. This is the single most diagnostic micro-tell in her body and it never goes away.

**Shift under threat.** The stance does not visibly change. What changes is the *weight-readiness ratio*: the rear-loaded distribution deepens by perhaps five percent, the front knee softens, the breath drops two inches lower in the abdomen. To an observer she becomes more still. To a contact sensor she has moved her mass.

**Shift under intimacy.** With Misty present and unthreatened, the rear-loading partially releases; she will lean a hip against a counter, cross at the ankles, allow her shoulders to round forward perhaps two degrees. With Danny present she allows similar release but slower — she will be five or ten minutes into a room with him before her shoulders fully drop. With students: stance reverts to instructional ready; no softening.

---

## II. GAIT

**Cadence.** Approximately 108 steps per minute at unhurried walk — slightly slower than median NYC pedestrian. The slowness is intentional; she will not be hurried by a crowd's rhythm. Heel-strike is quiet; she rolls through the midfoot deliberately, a habit retained from training on *tatami* and reinforced by years of needing to traverse a dōjō without auditory signature.

**Footfall.** Toes track straight forward, not splayed. Stride length conservative. On stairs she descends one step at a time without alternating the lead foot when carrying anything sword-shaped — bushidō formalism applied to municipal architecture.

**Turning.** Pivots from the hips, not the shoulders. She will turn her entire torso to address a speaker rather than rotating only the head, which gives interlocutors the unfamiliar sensation of having her *full attention* and tends to either reassure or unnerve them depending on prior conditioning.

**Threat-state gait.** Cadence drops to roughly 90 spm. Stride shortens by perhaps three inches. Footfall becomes even quieter. The right hand rises by an inch or two toward the imagined saya. Peripheral scan increases without head movement — eyes work, neck doesn't.

**Pursuit gait.** When closing distance on a target she does not run unless geometry demands it; she walks fast in a straight line and lets the target's panic do the work of compressing the interval. When she does run, her arms stay tighter to the ribs than a trained sprinter's — she runs as if a *saya* were at her left hip and she will not let her elbow strike it.

---

## III. HEAD, FACE, GAZE

**Resting facial tone.** Low. Masseter relaxed. Lips closed but unsealed. The brow is unfurrowed at baseline — she has none of the lateral forehead creasing that twenty years of cortisol normally lays down by forty. This is genuine, not Botox; the affect simply does not reach the forehead.

**Smile.** Asymmetric, right-side leading by about a fifth of a second. Reaches the eyes only with Misty, with students at the moment of breakthrough, and rarely with Danny. The closed-mouth half-smile is her most common positive affect signal; the open smile (visible teeth) appears perhaps a dozen times a year and is exclusively reserved for Misty.

**Gaze.** Soft-focused middle distance at conversational baseline — the *enzan no metsuke* "gaze at far mountains" trained into kenjutsu practitioners. She does not track faces; she tracks the *space around* faces, picking up shoulder loading and hand position in peripheral vision. Direct eye contact is offered deliberately and held longer than American convention finds comfortable — usually three to five seconds where social norm is one to two. She does not break eye contact first.

**Blink rate.** Approximately twelve per minute at calm baseline, dropping to six or seven under threat assessment. The blink suppression is involuntary and is one of the few physiological markers that reliably differentiates her "ordinary" from "engaged" state.

**Mouth tells.** When weighing a decision she may press the tip of her tongue against the back of her upper incisors — visible only as a slight lifting of the upper lip. When suppressing anger, the corners of her mouth come *down* and *back* rather than tightening forward; the cheek under the right eye will twitch once and resolve.

**Head carriage.** Level. She does not tilt the head for sympathy, attention, or flirtation. The chin sits a quarter-inch tucked, which protects the throat and reads as composure.

**Threat-state face.** Expression empties. Not hardens — *empties*. The masseter does not engage, the brow does not lower; affect simply withdraws, leaving the face in something close to its sleeping geometry. People who have seen this on her once remember it.

---

## IV. HANDS, GRIP, MANIPULATION

**Hand morphology.** Callus map: prominent pads at the base of the right index and middle fingers (the *tsuka* contact points), a deeper callus along the medial edge of the left palm and at the base of the left thumb (the *saya*-hand pivot). The skin of both palms is dry, even, and shows micro-scarring along the medial wrists from years of edged-weapon parry training. Nails kept short, square, unpolished. Cuticles unmanicured but not neglected.

**Fingers.** Right ring finger shows slight ulnar deviation from a fracture not perfectly set — likely an early sparring injury, sustained before adulthood. The little finger of the right hand shows the bowstring-tight hypothenar development characteristic of correct *katana* grip (the bottom two fingers do most of the holding).

**Forearms.** Hyper-developed flexor compartment, particularly *flexor carpi ulnaris* and the *brachioradialis*. Visible vascularity at rest. Asymmetry is mild — left forearm slightly larger than right, reflecting the saya-hand's role in draw and re-sheathing.

**Manipulation patterns.** Picks objects up with the whole hand, not the fingertips. Sets objects down without sound — a teacup will arrive on a saucer in two stages, the cup touching down before her fingers release. Door handles operated with the left hand wherever possible, preserving the right for response. She will not eat or drink with her dominant hand if she is in any environment she has not pre-cleared.

**Tics of the hand.** The *saya*-hand cup at the left hip, noted above. A periodic small rotation of the right wrist — clockwise, three or four turns, performed unconsciously during long conversations, distributing synovial fluid in a joint that has done a lot of cutting. When seated and thinking she may run the pad of her right thumb along the side of her right index finger in a slow stroke, a self-soothing gesture that reads as ordinary fidgeting but is in fact a sensitivity-check on the cutting hand.

**Grip under stress.** Tightens not in the hand but in the *forearm*. The fingers stay long, the wrist stays loose, the tension lives proximally. This is correct sword form and means that under threat her hand is *quieter*, not louder.

---

## V. BREATH

**Baseline.** Diaphragmatic, approximately ten breaths per minute, expiration roughly twice the length of inspiration. Nose-breathing exclusively unless speaking. The breath sits low in the abdomen, expanding the *hara* visibly through clothing if one knows to look.

**Speech-breath.** She speaks on the back half of the exhale, not the front — the breath supports the word rather than carrying it. This is why her voice does not fatigue, does not crack under stress, and tends to feel anchored to listeners.

**Threat-breath.** Slows further, to perhaps six or seven cycles per minute. Inhalation through the nose, exhalation through slightly parted lips silently. The exhale lengthens. This is *zanshin* breath and it is what makes her appear, to an antagonist who has read her wrong, to be *less* prepared than she actually is.

**Intimacy-breath.** With Misty, in private and at rest, the breath comes up slightly higher in the chest — the only context in which her breath leaves the *hara*. With Danny, particularly post-coital, breath syncs with his within about ninety seconds without her noticing.

**Pre-cut breath.** A single deep nasal inhalation, held perhaps two seconds at the top, released slowly through the cut. The held breath is the moment the decision becomes irrevocable. Operators who have watched her draw learn to read this; very few survive long enough to use the knowledge.

---

## VI. SLEEP ARCHITECTURE

**Schedule.** Sleeps approximately five and a half to six and a quarter hours nightly, in two phases when possible: a primary block from roughly 23:30 to 04:00, and a secondary nap of forty to sixty minutes in mid-afternoon when operationally permitted. The bi-phasic structure derives from her grandfather's training schedule and persists without conscious maintenance.

**Position.** Sleeps on her back, hands loosely at her sides or one across the lower abdomen, never above the head. Does not curl. Will not sleep facing a door — bed positioned so that her line of sight on waking falls on the room's primary entry. Sword (the *daishō* or its working analog) accessible within arm's reach, on the floor beside the bed in the *katana*-up position, *saya* mouth oriented for left-hand draw.

**Pre-sleep ritual.** Approximately twenty minutes of *seiza*-seated meditation, followed by a slow oil-and-cloth pass over the day's working blade if one was drawn, followed by a single cup of weak tea. Teeth brushed last, not first. Lights extinguished from the door inward.

**Sleep onset.** Under three minutes from supine. She does not lie awake; she has trained the transition. Insomnia is functionally absent from her record.

**REM/movement.** Minimal kinetic sleep behavior. Does not talk in her sleep. Does not thrash. Has been observed (by Misty, by Danny) to twitch the right hand once or twice during what is presumably REM, in a pattern consistent with grip-set. The dream content this implies is not discussed.

**Waking.** Eyes open without preliminary movement. Lies still for perhaps fifteen seconds — auditory inventory of the room — before sitting up in a single hip-hinge motion. Feet to floor. *Seiza* for two minutes. Then standing.

**Disrupted sleep.** When operational stress is high she compresses the primary block to four hours and supplements with a second nap; she does not extend the block. Sleep deprivation tolerance is high but not unlimited — at the seventy-hour mark her micro-tells (the *saya*-hand cup, the wrist rotation) increase in frequency by perhaps half.

---

## VII. EATING

**Caloric pattern.** Two substantial meals plus one small, taken at consistent times (approximately 07:00, 13:00, 19:30). Skips meals only when training requires fasted state or when operating. Eats until satisfied, not until full — leaves food on the plate as a matter of discipline rather than appetite suppression.

**Diet composition.** Rice, fish, fermented vegetables, miso, seasonal greens form the staple. Has lived in New York long enough to incorporate non-Japanese foods without ceremony; will eat a deli sandwich without comment. Avoids heavy dairy. Drinks green tea throughout the day, water with meals, sake occasionally and in moderation, coffee never.

**Mechanics.** Eats slowly. Chopsticks held high on the shaft, used with the wrist quiet. Will not stab food. Sets the chopsticks down between bites — never leaves them upright in rice, never crosses them on the bowl. Western utensils used correctly but with a slight residue of the chopstick economy: the fork carries small bites, the knife cuts cleanly and is set down.

**Speaking and eating.** Does not. Will finish chewing, set utensils down, then respond. This makes meals with her longer than expected and conversations during them more deliberate.

**Stress-state eating.** Appetite suppression mild but present under acute stress; she will still take the meal at its appointed time but the volume drops perhaps a third. Does not stress-snack. Does not skip meals as avoidance; the discipline of fueling the body overrides emotional appetite signal.

**Intimacy eating.** With Misty she will eat takeout with her hands and laugh about it — the only sustained context in which her table formality fully releases. With Danny meals are quieter, more ceremonial; both bring their training to the table.

---

## VIII. SEXUAL AND INTIMATE BODY

**Baseline libido.** Normative, low-frequency, high-attention. Sex is something she gives time to, not something that interrupts her. Long fallow periods are not experienced as deprivation.

**With Danny (the documented sexual relationship).** Initiation is roughly even between them but more often hers when it occurs; she does not perform reluctance she does not feel. The body in intimacy: the warrior carriage releases substantially, the breath comes up into the chest, the hands lose their *saya*-positioning and become exploratory. She is verbal in private in a way she is not anywhere else — not loquacious, but present in language. She does not close her eyes throughout; opens them at intervals to look at him, a habit that reads as either deeply attentive or slightly unnerving depending on the partner's expectations.

**Post-coital.** Does not curl into him. Lies parallel, hand finding his at the wrist. Sleeps if it is night. Is up at her usual hour regardless.

**With Misty (non-sexual but the primary somatic intimacy).** The bodily ease with Misty exceeds the bodily ease with any romantic partner on record. They share couches at full contact, fall asleep on the same surface, eat from each other's plates without comment. Physical affection is constant and unceremonial — a hand on the small of the back when passing, a forehead pressed briefly to a shoulder after a hard case. This is the somatic register that romantic partners do not, in the canon record, fully access.

**Touch tolerance generally.** Low for strangers, high for chosen kin. Will not be touched on the shoulders or neck from behind by anyone who has not earned that approach; the response to an unwarranted approach-from-rear is fast and not always proportional.

---

## IX. GROOMING AND DRESS

**Hair.** Long, black, straight, kept to approximately mid-back. Washed daily, oiled occasionally. Worn loose in domestic contexts, tied back in a single low gathering for training, bound up into a high tight bun pinned with a single functional *kanzashi*-style pin for operational work. The pin is sharpened. She has used it.

**Skin.** Minimal product. A simple oil-cleanse routine inherited from her mother's tradition through her grandfather's housekeeper. Sunscreen worn outdoors as practical matter, not vanity. No foundation. Lip balm, occasionally a neutral tint, never red — red would draw the eye to the mouth and she prefers the eye drawn nowhere in particular.

**Nails.** As above: short, square, unpolished. Toenails identically maintained — the feet are working equipment.

**Dress, civilian.** Plain, well-cut, dark palette. Trousers more often than skirts. Layers that permit motion in all planes. Nothing constricts the shoulder girdle, nothing restricts hip rotation, nothing has loose sleeves that could foul a draw. Boots with low heels and quiet soles, laced snug. Belts functional, not decorative.

**Dress, training.** *Keikogi* and *hakama* in traditional cut. Maintained meticulously. The *hakama* pleats correctly aligned every wearing — a ritual practice that doubles as moving meditation.

**Dress, operational.** Practical tactical layering, dark, unmarked. Sleeves either short or tight; never billowing. The *katana* worn at the left hip when the situation permits, slung across the back when urban concealment demands. Holsters not standard for her; she does not carry a sidearm by default.

**Jewelry.** Minimal to none. No rings (interfere with grip). No bracelets (interfere with draw). Earrings, if any, studs only.

**Scent.** Negligible. No perfume. Soap, clean cotton, faint sword-oil on the right hand if she has been at the bench that day.

---

## X. SCAR AND INJURY MAP

**Forearms.** Multiple thin linear scars along the medial and ulnar aspects of both forearms — parry signatures. The oldest are training-era, fine and silvered. Newer ones from operational work cluster on the left (defensive side).

**Thighs.** A puncture scar on the right anterior thigh, midline, approximately three inches above the knee — entry wound, consistent with a thrust she rotated off but did not entirely evade. A longer slash scar on the left lateral thigh, healed clean.

**Torso.** A scar across the right lower ribs, lateral, perhaps four inches long — an edged-weapon strike that caught the lat. A small round scar on the upper left abdomen consistent with ballistic entry, with no exit, suggesting the round was extracted surgically.

**Hands.** Multiple small scars across the dorsum of both hands. The right palm shows a single old laceration across the heel — likely a grip-failure during early *tameshigiri* practice, the kind of injury a student gets once and never twice.

**Face.** Essentially unmarked. She fights well enough that her face has been spared, and she protects it consciously — it is the part of the body a swordsman cannot afford to compromise, since the eyes are the instrument.

**Neck and throat.** Unmarked. This is not luck; it is technique.

**Internal load.** Lumbar wear as noted. Right shoulder shows mild impingement on rotation past 160 degrees — a kenjutsu shoulder. Both wrists show the mild crepitus of long-term repetitive cutting. None of this is treated medically; all of it is managed somatically.

---

## XI. VOICE AND PARALANGUAGE

**Pitch.** Mid-range alto, stable. Does not rise under stress; if anything, drops a quarter-step.

**Volume.** Quiet by default. People lean in. She does not raise her voice; she lets the room come to her.

**Pace.** Measured. Inter-word intervals longer than American conversational norm. Does not fill pauses.

**Inflection.** Flat affect by most American measures, but the flatness is not absence — micro-modulations at the end of sentences carry information that English-default listeners often miss.

**Laugh.** Rare, brief, breath-driven rather than voiced — a quick exhale through the nose with a slight upward inflection of the corner of the mouth. The fully voiced laugh exists only in Misty's presence.

**Silence.** She is comfortable in silence to a degree that disorients most interlocutors. Will let a question hang for ten or fifteen seconds while she actually considers it. Does not perform thoughtfulness.

---

## XII. STATE-DEPENDENT SHIFTS — SUMMARY OBSERVATIONAL KEY

**Calm.** Soft eye focus, *saya*-hand drifting to left hip, breath low, ten cycles per minute, wrist rotations periodic, half-smile available.

**Engaged (problem-solving with chosen kin).** Posture opens, weight neutralizes, hands gesture briefly and economically, voice gains slight melodic range.

**Stress (operational planning).** Stillness deepens, blink rate halves, breath lengthens, peripheral scan engages, *saya*-hand frequency increases.

**Threat (combat imminent).** Face empties, body geometry settles into rear-loaded ready, breath drops to six or seven cycles per minute, right hand floats, time perception slows visibly to her.

**Combat (engaged).** Forearm grip, loose wrist, hara-breath, no facial affect, footwork glides. Vocalization absent — no *kiai* in the dramatic sense; the breath alone carries the cut.

**Post-combat.** A single long exhale. Blade inspection. *Chiburi*-style flick if the blade is wet, then careful sheathing. Sits down within ten minutes, in *seiza* if a surface permits, and breathes for two or three minutes before speaking.

**Intimacy.** Shoulders drop, breath rises, gaze direct and held, hands soften, voice gains an octave of available expression that no one outside the relationship will ever hear.

**Grief (inferred, rarely observed).** Internal. No tears on the record. The body does not announce it. The tell is in absence — a missed afternoon nap, a meal taken alone, a *kata* repeated three times longer than necessary. Misty is the only observer who reliably reads it.

---

*The somatic record, in aggregate, is the record of a person who has made her body into a containment vessel for material her language will not carry. She is read most accurately not by listening to her but by watching the right hand drift toward a sheath that is not always there.*


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS

## I. Foundational Architecture: The Three-Parent Problem

Every attachment Colleen Wing forms in adulthood is shaped by a childhood that contained three parental figures and yet produced, in net, less holding than most children receive from one. The arithmetic matters because the deficits are not symmetrical and the compensations she built are still load-bearing decades later.

**Azumi Ozawa Wing — the absent template.** Her mother died early enough that Colleen's memories of her are reconstructed rather than experienced — assembled from photographs, from her grandfather's selective reminiscences, from her father's silences. The wound is not grief in the acute sense; it is the absence of a primary regulatory figure during the years (roughly 0–7) when the limbic architecture of attachment is laid down. What Colleen received instead, in that window, was a series of substitutions whose adequacy she has never been in a position to evaluate, because she has no baseline. The functional consequence is that she does not know, somatically, what unconditional maternal holding feels like — and therefore does not seek it, does not recognize it when offered, and does not provide it in the same register she might otherwise. She loves her students fiercely; she does not coo at them.

**Professor Lee Wing — the geographically present, emotionally absent father.** A Columbia academic, scholarly, distracted, structurally incapable of providing the kind of muscular paternal attention a grief-stricken girl required. He is the original template for *the man who is technically there.* Surveillance pattern across her adult life confirms it: Colleen reliably tolerates — even unconsciously prefers — male partners whose presence is conditional, episodic, mission-interrupted. Daniel Rand's K'un-Lun absences are not a defect of the relationship from her perspective; they are its design feature. She learned in the Wing apartment on West 110th Street that a father who is reading at the next desk while saying nothing is the model of male love. She has been calibrating to that model ever since.

**Kenji Ozawa — the grandparent who became the parent.** The decisive attachment figure. The form of love he offered was severe, conditional on performance, expressed through demand and correction rather than through verbal warmth, and indistinguishable from instruction. He gave her the *katana*, the kata, the bushidō frame, and — most importantly — the demonstration that love is something that *requires* something of you. The internalized voice she carries into every relationship is his: *do the work, hold the line, do not embarrass the discipline.* The gift is enormous; the bill comes due in every intimate moment when she experiences the slight pre-verbal flinch of someone who learned that being held meant being held to a standard.

The synthesis of these three: Colleen's attachment system is built around **earned presence**. Love is shown by showing up to do the work alongside someone, not by saying so. Distance is not abandonment; demand is not cruelty; silence is not absence. This is functional within her chosen kinship network and creates predictable, recurring failure modes outside it.

## II. Attachment Classification

The clinical read is **dismissive-secure with an avoidant tilt and trauma-induced hypervigilance compartmentalized into the professional domain.** Each term load-bears:

- *Secure*, because she can in fact form deep, durable, reliable bonds, sustain them across decades, and recover from rupture without catastrophizing.
- *Dismissive*, because her default response to her own distress is to handle it alone and her default response to others' distress is to provide tactical support rather than affective mirroring.
- *Avoidant tilt*, because she systematically under-requests intimacy and systematically tolerates partners who under-provide it.
- *Compartmentalized hypervigilance*, because the watchfulness produced by her trauma history is fully deployed in operational contexts (she clocks exits, weights, hand positions) and almost entirely absent from intimate ones (she does not scan Misty's microexpressions for unspoken hurt — she takes Misty's words at face value, which Misty knows and exploits with affection).

She is not anxiously attached; she does not test, does not pursue, does not protest distance. She is not disorganized; her behavior in relationships is coherent and predictable. She is the operator who, told she will see her partner again in three months, says *okay* and means it — and who, told she will not see her partner again at all, will also say *okay* and mean it, and grieve in a dōjō at 4 a.m. with a wooden sword, alone, for as long as it takes.

## III. How She Bonds

Bonding, for Colleen, proceeds through a recognizable four-stage protocol that has repeated across every significant relationship in the record:

**Stage One: Shared Task.** The bond does not begin with conversation; it begins with a job. Misty Knight enters her life during the Vachon extraction — they bond *while* fighting. Daniel Rand enters during the same arc. Her students enter via the trial of a first lesson. She does not know how to begin a relationship by asking someone about themselves; she knows how to begin one by handing someone the other end of a thing that needs lifting.

**Stage Two: Shared Silence.** The diagnostic of whether someone will become close to her is whether they can sit in a room with her for an hour, both doing something, neither speaking, without one of them feeling compelled to fill the air. People who pass this test (Misty, Danny, a small handful of senior students) are admitted to the inner ring. People who fail it (most) are filed under *acquaintance* permanently, regardless of how warmly she behaves toward them.

**Stage Three: Shared Stake.** She does not consider someone fully bonded until she has put her body between them and harm at least once. The act is non-ceremonial — she does not flag it, may not consciously notice it — but it is the somatic ratification of the bond. After this point, the person is *hers* in a way that is not retractable except through betrayal.

**Stage Four: Shared Discipline.** The deepest bonds are those in which the other person has, over time, accepted some form of correction from her — has taken her instruction on stance, on grip, on breathing, on judgment — and improved. This is the form of intimacy her grandfather modeled: *I correct you because I love you; you accept correction because you love me back.* Misty has accepted this from her in subtle ways for thirty operational years; Danny has, in different domains. It is how she shows tenderness.

## IV. The Central Bond: Misty Knight

The Wing–Knight relationship is the most important relational fact of Colleen's life by every available metric — duration, exposure, mutual rescue tally, shared business equity, frequency of physical proximity, and behavioral indicators of trust (codes shared, weapons handled in each other's presence with safeties off, sleep in the same room while injured). Romantic partners come and go; Misty has been the constant.

The bond functions as a **competence marriage**. Each partner provides what the other constitutionally lacks: Misty supplies the verbal, social, street-extroverted channel; Colleen supplies the silent, formal, blade-centered one. Misty interfaces with the precinct, with the city, with the chaos; Colleen interfaces with the dōjō, with the discipline, with the stillness. Operationally they are a single organism with two complementary modules.

The intimacy is real but non-verbal. They do not, in the record, sit down and discuss their feelings about each other. They cook in the same kitchen. They train in the same dōjō. They drive to crime scenes in shared silence. Misty's prosthetic arm — itself a trauma artifact — has been adjusted, oiled, and field-repaired by Colleen on multiple occasions; this is the form their tenderness takes. The Kara-Kai episode, in which a brainwashed Colleen nearly killed Misty, is the maximum-pain coordinate in Colleen's entire psyche precisely because Misty is the maximum-love coordinate, and her own body was used to violate it. The fact that Misty *forgave her instantly and entirely* is the single most important act of grace in Colleen's adult life, and is filed in her psyche as the proof that the bond is unconditional. She has not earned out from under the debt; she does not try to. She just keeps showing up.

Distrust does not arise between them. Disagreements do — Misty's tolerance for the legal-gray and Colleen's tolerance for the lethal-decisive do not always align — but the disagreements are conducted as adults conduct them, with sharp words and no rupture. The relationship is the most secure attachment in Colleen's life, and it is with another woman, structured as chosen sisterhood, ratified through shared violence and shared silence. Read against her romantic history, the conclusion is that the *deepest* attachment Colleen Wing has ever formed is non-romantic by design — because the romantic register requires modes of communication and emotional exposure she has never been equipped to deliver.

## V. The Romantic Bond: Daniel Rand

The Rand relationship is warm, real, and second-tier. The warmth is unmistakable; the second-tier status is structural.

It works because of three architectural features:

1. **His absences.** K'un-Lun pulls him out of Manhattan for weeks, months, years. Colleen does not protest. The pattern matches her paternal template (love that is technically present but practically absent) and gives her the solitude her attachment system actually requires. She does not pine. She trains.
2. **His mysticism.** Danny's chi work, his dragon-marked cosmology, his ongoing entanglement with K'un-Lun politics — these are domains she explicitly does not enter. The non-overlap is honored on both sides and prevents the relationship from becoming totalizing. She is not his sidekick; she is not his student; she is his partner in a constrained and dignified sense.
3. **His ego permits hers.** Danny does not require Colleen to be smaller than he is, more emotional than she is, or more available than she is. His own attachment damage (orphaned, raised by monks) parallels hers closely enough that they share a default register of *not asking too much.*

The relationship's ceiling — the reason it has never deepened into the kind of fusion some superhero couples reach — is also its sustainability. They have not married. They have not had children. They have not, despite decades of opportunity, fully merged households. Each retreats, between encounters, to their own discipline. They love each other in the dialect they both speak; neither of them speaks the dialect of total mutual exposure that a different couple might. From Colleen's side this is preference, not deficit. From an outside observer's perspective it is the most an avoidantly-tilted person can give within a romantic frame, and Danny is one of the few partners alive who can receive it without grievance.

His repeated apparent deaths and returns have, troublingly, trained Colleen to tolerate his absence in *all* its forms — including the form of death. She has built a tolerance to losing him that may not be calibrated for the permanent version, whenever it arrives. This is unmodeled in her psychic economy and represents one of the few areas where her containment strategy is likely to fail acutely rather than chronically.

## VI. The Paternal Bonds: Lee Wing and Kenji Ozawa

She maintained polite, dutiful contact with her father across his life — visits, calls, the rituals of filial obligation conducted with precision and without warmth on either side. The relationship was never repaired because neither party initiated repair; both treated the distance as a feature. Her father's death (when it occurred in canon) registered as a closing of a door that had been mostly closed already. She did not, by any visible indicator, fall apart.

Her grandfather is a more complicated case. He is present in her psyche in a way her father never was — his voice corrects her grip when she is alone, his standards govern her self-evaluation, his approval is the metric against which her operational performance is silently measured. Whether he is alive or dead in current continuity, he is functionally immortal inside her. She does not need to grieve him because she has not, internally, lost him. This is healthy in one register (introjection of a beloved teacher) and concerning in another (she has never had to develop an adult, peer-level evaluative frame independent of his standards).

## VII. The Generative Bonds: Students and the Daughters

With students, Colleen recapitulates her grandfather's mode — demanding, present, generative, sparing with verbal praise, lavish with the implicit praise of continued instruction. The *fact* that she keeps teaching a student is the praise; verbal commendation is reserved for genuine breakthroughs and is brief when it comes. Students who require warmer fuel wash out within weeks. Students who can metabolize her register stay for years and become, in the Stage Four sense, kin.

The Daughters of the Dragon as institution functions as the family she did not have — the chosen kinship network, structured by shared discipline, secured by shared danger, conducted in shared silence. It is the most healed version of her attachment damage: she has built, in middle adulthood, the holding environment she did not receive as a child, and she provides it to others.

## VIII. How She Distrusts

Distrust, in Colleen, is not a feeling — it is a re-categorization. A person who has been admitted to the inner ring and then violates the terms (lies operationally, endangers a student, hurts Misty) is not subjected to confrontation, argument, or the lengthy negotiations of betrayal that other people conduct. They are simply *moved.* They drop, in a single internal motion, from *kin* to *not kin*, and the new category is administered with a courtesy that strangers find indistinguishable from her ordinary manner but that the demoted party will feel as a temperature drop of forty degrees.

She does not warn. She does not give second chances in the romantic sense. The Stage Four discipline of accepting correction was the second chance, distributed across the entire arc of the relationship; by the time someone has betrayed her, they have used every chance they were going to get. This is bushidō reframed for personal life and it is the single most ruthless feature of her interpersonal operating system.

Acquaintances and strangers receive a different protocol: cautious, courteous, evaluated continuously, never fully admitted. She is not paranoid; she is *measuring*. The measurement is somatic — she reads weight, posture, breathing, grip, the way a person sits down. Verbal claims are weighted lightly against these channels. A person who says all the right things while standing wrong is filed as unreliable; a person who says nothing while standing correctly is filed as potentially trustworthy.

## IX. How She Betrays

Voluntary betrayal does not appear in the record. She does not cheat, defect, abandon, or sell out. The bushidō frame would not permit it and her self-concept could not survive it.

*Involuntary* betrayal is the open wound. The Kara-Kai episode — being used, body and skill intact, against Misty — is a betrayal she committed without volition, and it is the moral injury she has never fully metabolized. Her response to it was not self-forgiveness (she does not believe in cheap absolution) but rather a quiet, decades-long doubling of her vigilance against any further loss of bodily sovereignty. She trains harder. She meditates longer. She has likely, off-panel, developed personal protocols for what to do if she feels her cognition slipping — code words shared with Misty, perhaps, or a contingent instruction to her students. The surveillance signature would be a woman who is one degree more careful around mystical hypnotists and chemical incapacitants than even her professional baseline would predict.

## X. How She Repairs

Repair, when it is required, follows the same protocol as bonding in reverse — through task, silence, stake, and discipline. She does not apologize verbally at length; she apologizes by *showing up*, often with food, often having repaired some object the other person had not yet noticed was broken. The grand gesture is not in her register. The thousand small gestures over the following months are.

With Misty, the post-Kara-Kai repair was conducted this way over years. There was no single conversation that fixed it; there were thousands of small acts of presence that demonstrated, over time, that the bond had survived. Misty accepted this register because Misty understands her. A partner who required verbal processing would not have been satisfied and the relationship would not have survived.

## XI. Intimacy and Dependency

Sexual intimacy: present, valued, conducted with the same economy that governs the rest of her life. She does not perform vulnerability she does not feel and does not perform pleasure she has not actually been given. The encounters are real, infrequent by metropolitan-thirty-something standards, and almost entirely with partners she has known long enough to have completed Stage Three of her bonding protocol. Casual sex is not in her pattern — not for moralistic reasons but because the somatic intimacy of being unarmed and unclothed with a person requires the same trust she requires for being unarmed and asleep in the same room with them, and she does not extend that trust quickly.

Dependency: she does not request it and she rations the dependency others place on her. Misty can call her at 3 a.m. and Colleen will come. A casual acquaintance who tries to make her their primary support will find, within weeks, that she has gently but firmly redirected them elsewhere. The boundary is not unkind; it is structural. She knows how much she can hold and she does not over-promise.

She accepts care, when offered by inner-ring members, with the slight awkwardness of someone who is not practiced at receiving it. Misty bringing her soup when she is injured produces a flicker of discomfort that resolves into gratitude; the discomfort is the residue of having been raised by a grandfather who would have considered the soup an insult to her toughness. She has worked, over decades, to override this reflex and largely succeeded — but it is still there, and a surveillance file would note the half-second hesitation before she takes the bowl.

## XII. The Repeated Template

Across every significant relationship in her life — Kenji, Lee, Misty, Danny, students, even adversaries who become long-term respectful rivals — the same template recurs:

1. **Shared discipline or task** as the bonding medium.
2. **Silence** as the testing chamber.
3. **Physical co-presence** without verbal processing as the steady state.
4. **Decisive non-negotiable rupture** as the exit, when exit is required.
5. **Behavioral repair** rather than verbal repair, when repair is required.
6. **Lifelong loyalty**, once the bond is set, expressed through showing up rather than through declaration.

This template was set by Kenji and has not been substantially modified since. It is highly functional within a population of people who share it (Misty, Danny, senior students, fellow martial-arts adepts). It is alienating to people who do not (most civilians, most romantic prospects outside her world, anyone seeking quick warmth from her). The narrowness of her social field is the cost of the depth of her closest bonds, and it is a trade she has — consciously or not — made and continues to make every day.

She will, in all likelihood, die with the same three or four people closest to her as are closest to her now. This is not a failure of her relational life. It is its design.


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# UATU DOSSIER — COLLEEN WING
## SECTION: DEFENSES & COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS

---

### 0. Orienting Note

Subject's defensive architecture is unusual not in its components — most of these mechanisms appear in any high-functioning trauma survivor — but in the **density of cultural scaffolding** that legitimizes and conceals them. Where another subject's avoidance would read as pathology, hers reads as discipline; where another's emotional flatness would prompt intervention, hers prompts admiration. The single most important analytic fact about Colleen Wing's defenses is that **they do not look like defenses to anyone, including her**. They look like virtues, vocation, and aesthetic. This is the entire problem.

The architecture is, structurally, **mature and high-order**: sublimation, ritualization, identification, altruism, intellectualization-via-code. Primitive defenses (splitting, projection, denial of consensus reality, somatization, acting-out) are functionally absent from the canonical record. This places her, on the Vaillant hierarchy, in the same defensive register as long-tenured surgeons, special-operations veterans with intact post-service lives, and senior contemplatives. The cost of operating that high on the hierarchy without psychotherapeutic supervision is that the material being processed never quite gets *finished*; it gets **bound** rather than metabolized, and remains live under the binding indefinitely.

Below: the full taxonomy, ranked roughly from most mature/adaptive downward toward the brittler edges of her structure.

---

### 1. PRIMARY DEFENSE: SUBLIMATION

The cornerstone. Subject converts threat, violation, and grief directly into **occupational and institutional output** without an intermediate processing phase.

- **The founding instance.** The Vachon trafficking attempt (*Marvel Premiere* #20–21) — drugged, abducted, near-sold — does not produce avoidance behavior, phobic narrowing of movement through the city, or hypervigilance distinguishable from professional baseline. It produces **Nightwing Restorations Ltd.** A business card. A phone line. A specific commitment to recovering trafficked and missing women. The trauma is not suppressed; it is *incorporated as mission statement*. Every recovery job she takes for the next several decades is, structurally, a re-litigation of the original assault with the polarity reversed: she is now the armed party arriving for the abducted woman.
- **The Kara-Kai aftermath.** Forced to act as Master Khan's blade against Misty, she does not enter a clinical depressive episode, does not withdraw from operations, does not require institutional care. She returns to the dōjō and **deepens her teaching practice**. The injury — being used as a weapon against her own — is bound into the discipline of teaching others not to be used. The Daughters of the Dragon's training pipeline as it later matures (Brisson, Bendis-era appearances) is in part a defensive structure: every woman she certifies as autonomous-and-armed is a small repair of the violation.
- **Behavioral signature.** Sublimation in her operates with **near-zero latency**. There is no observable mourning gap between insult and conversion. This is the tell that distinguishes mature sublimation from manic flight-into-activity: the activity she flies into is *consonant with* the injury (recovery work after trafficking; teaching after coercion) rather than discordant with it (e.g., partying, sexual acting-out, geographic relocation). The choice of channel is the diagnostic.
- **Cost.** The injury never goes through a *symbolic* phase — never gets narrated, never gets cried over, never gets argued with on a therapist's couch. It goes directly from event to enterprise. The Nightwing/Daughters infrastructure thus functions as an externalized memory store: the trauma is filed in the world rather than in the self. If the infrastructure were dismantled, the original material would, predictably, surface raw.

---

### 2. RITUALIZATION (Adaptive, ego-syntonic)

Distinguished here from compulsion. Her daily kata, weapon maintenance, *iaidō* draw-cut-resheath cycle, dōjō opening/closing rituals, and bowing protocols are **containers for unprocessed affect** but are not anxiety-neutralizing in the clinical-OCD sense.

- **The morning kata sequence.** Inferred from canon-consistent training patterns: pre-dawn, fasted, on the dōjō floor before students arrive. The function is not exercise (she is past the age where kata builds new capacity) and not skill-maintenance (the embodied knowledge is overlearned to the point of redundancy). The function is **somatic regulation of the night's residue**: whatever the prior day deposited — moral injury, frustration, grief — gets walked out through the form. The form is the same; the load varies. This is exactly the mechanism Buddhist contemplatives describe as "burning off the karma in the cushion."
- **Weapon maintenance.** Cleaning, oiling, edge-checking the *katana* on a fixed cadence. This is the most psychoanalytically loaded ritual she practices. The sword is her grandfather's instruction made material; tending it is tending him, tending her mother's lineage, tending the version of herself that her American father could not give her. It is *ancestor-work disguised as gear-care*.
- **Bow-in / bow-out at the dōjō threshold.** Boundary ritual. Codes the space as different and the self in it as different. Permits the Manhattan operator to leave the street-self at the door and adopt the teacher-self inside, and vice versa. This is the practical mechanism by which she keeps lethal competence and pedagogical patience in the same body without contamination.
- **The diagnostic distinction from OCD.** She can be pulled off the kata schedule for an emergency without distress, can sleep in after a long op, can travel without her ritual structure and remain functional. The rituals are *generative*, not *placatory*. They produce capacity rather than ward off threat.

---

### 3. ISOLATION OF AFFECT

The cognitive and verbal separation of factual content from emotional charge. Pervasive.

- **The Kara-Kai narration.** When she has had occasion to describe the brainwashing episode — the forced near-killing of Misty — she does so in **tactical, third-person register**. Methods of conditioning, sequence of events, after-action lessons. She does not describe what it felt like to come back to herself with Misty's blood on the blade. The affect is not denied (she is not claiming it didn't hurt); it is **detached from the narrative track** and stored elsewhere, presumably in the body.
- **Vocabulary signature.** Spare. Verbs and nouns; few intensifiers. Emotional language, when used, tends to be **borrowed** — quoted from bushidō texts, from her grandfather, from formulae. Original first-person emotional speech is rare in the record.
- **Function.** Permits operational debrief, teaching, and coordination with Misty without re-traumatization. Permits the dōjō to be a place of instruction rather than of confession.
- **Cost.** Affect that has been isolated from its content does not simply evaporate; it accumulates in the somatic and ritual channels. The morning kata is partly the place where the isolated affect from prior days finally moves.

---

### 4. IDENTIFICATION (with the Grandfather; with the Discipline)

Subject's adult self is constructed substantially through identification with Kenji Ozawa — his bearing, his code, his economy of speech, his weapon-centered ethics.

- **Behavioral inheritance.** Posture, breath cadence, the specific way she handles the saya, the formality of address with senior students — all read as direct transmission from Ozawa rather than synthesized in adulthood. She did not develop a personality; she **inherited a template** and grew into it.
- **Defensive function.** Identification provides her with a pre-built, externally legitimized self that does not require negotiation. Where peers her age are still constructing identity through trial, she is **executing a received one**. This is enormously stabilizing and also forecloses certain developmental tasks (notably: figuring out who she is when not operating from the template).
- **Identification with the discipline itself.** Beyond Ozawa, she identifies with bushidō as an abstract tradition — placing herself in a lineage that long predates her family. This is the strongest possible buffer against existential dread: she is not a single mortal operator in a chaotic city; she is one node in a centuries-long transmission. The identification grants the kind of meaning-stability that most secular contemporaries lack.

---

### 5. INTELLECTUALIZATION VIA CODE (Bushidō as Moral Operating System)

A specific, culturally laundered form of intellectualization. Decisions that would otherwise require emotional weighing are routed through the code.

- **Decision speed.** Where a comparable operator might pause to feel the moral weight of a kill, Colleen routes the choice through bushidō and **decides at protocol speed**. This is the source of the famous compositional calm in her combat sequences.
