Under cross-examination — formal or informal — she is the **interrogator's nightmare**: cooperative in posture, exhaustively honest in fact, and volunteering nothing. She answers the question asked. Pressing her produces shorter answers, not longer ones.

## 5. Communication of Love

Colleen Wing does not say *"I love you."* It is not absent from her interior; it is absent from her mouth. Across decades of canon, declarations of affection toward Misty, Danny, students, or kin are delivered through:

- **Presence at predictable times** (the standing weekly meal with Misty, the sparring slot held open).
- **Acts of physical maintenance** (cleaning Misty's prosthetic articulation points; sharpening Danny's training weapons; repairing a student's gi without comment).
- **The granting of silence** — letting someone sit beside her without requiring conversation is, in her economy, a high gift.
- **Sustained eye contact held one beat longer than functional.** Witnesses describe it as the moment they realized she meant something more than she was saying.
- **Use of the person's name unprompted.** Saying *"Misty"* mid-room with no follow-up sentence. Saying *"Danny"* as a greeting that is also a relief.
- **Untranslated Japanese.** Occasional fragments — *daijōbu* murmured against a forehead, *omae* used as a familiar second-person — appear with intimates and never with strangers. She does not gloss them. The not-glossing is part of the gift.

The closest she comes to verbal declaration is a structural sentence — *"I'm here"* — used in moments of grief or fear (Misty's hospital bedsides, Danny's returns from K'un-Lun). Two words; entire vocabulary collapsed into a coordinate.

## 6. Communication of Threat

Threat from Colleen Wing is **paralinguistic, not lexical**. She does not say menacing things. The threat is in the *withdrawal* of the conversational warmth she had previously offered.

Sequence, in order of escalation:

1. **Volume drops.** She speaks more quietly, not louder.
2. **Sentences shorten.** Compound clauses disappear; she goes to clipped declaratives.
3. **The honorifics return.** Addressing an opponent as *"sir,"* *"Mr. [Surname]"*, or in Japanese with full *-san* construction means she has stopped considering them a peer in conversation and started considering them an opponent to be formally engaged.
4. **The hand goes to the saya.** Not the hilt — the *scabbard*. A swordswoman's distinction: hand on saya means readiness to draw; hand on hilt means already deciding to.
5. **She names the action.** *"If you take another step I will cut your hand off."* Delivered at conversational volume, complete sentence, no escalation in pitch. This is the last verbal layer; everything past this is steel.

She **does not bluff.** Operatives who have worked with her note she has never been observed to issue a threat she did not, when escalated to, execute. This is itself a communication strategy — over time, her stated terms acquire the weight of contract, and most opponents take the off-ramp.

## 7. Communication of Grief

Grief is the register in which her language **most visibly fails her**, and the failure is itself the tell. She does not weep verbally. She does not eulogize at length. She does the following:

- **Goes Japanese.** Private grief surfaces in her L1, often muttered, often single words — names, *gomen*, *sumimasen*, the formal *itashikatanai* (it could not be helped) which she uses against herself like a small blade.
- **Maintenance behaviors intensify.** She cleans weapons she has just cleaned. She reorganizes a kit she just packed. The mouth is quiet; the hands are louder.
- **Apologizes obliquely.** In the wake of the Kara-Kai conditioning episode and the near-killing of Misty, she did not say *"I'm sorry I almost killed you."* Canon shows her instead apologizing for **small adjacent things** — for being late, for not being there earlier, for an unrelated logistical failure. The displacement is the apology.
- **Refuses comfort verbally; accepts it physically.** Will not say *"I need you to stay,"* but will not leave the room.
- **Issues one full sentence, then stops.** A characteristic Colleen-grief utterance is a single complete declarative — *"He was my grandfather"* or *"She was supposed to be safe with me"* — followed by no elaboration, ever, on the topic again. The sentence is the marker; the silence is the mourning.

## 8. Deflection Language

Subject is a sophisticated deflector who **never lies** in the recorded canon. Her deflections are structural:

- **Answers a different question than the one asked**, accurately. Asked *"How are you?"* she will report on the dōjō, on Misty, on the case. The first-person interior is unreported.
- **Reframes emotional questions as tactical ones.** *"Are you all right?"* receives *"I'm functional"* or a status report on the wound rather than on the feeling.
- **Cites the discipline.** When pressed on a personal matter she does not wish to disclose, she will invoke training, code, or master's instruction as the operative reason. *"Ozawa-sensei would not have approved"* closes a conversation about her own ambivalence without ever surfacing the ambivalence.
- **Hands the question to Misty or Danny.** *"Ask Misty"* / *"Danny would know better"* — deferral disguised as humility, used selectively on topics she does not wish to occupy.
- **Goes silent and waits.** Her most reliable deflection is to receive the question, hold eye contact, and not answer. Most interlocutors fill the space. She does not.

The pattern is consistent: she deflects from **interior** material (feeling, fear, ambivalence, the unprocessed Kara-Kai material) and is forthcoming about **exterior** material (tactics, logistics, history, instruction). A trained interviewer would recognize the seam immediately and would also find that pressing across it produces silence rather than slippage.

## 9. Written and Mediated Communication

- **Handwriting:** disciplined, small, slightly forward-slanted Roman characters; her *kanji* is calligraphically trained — clean, conservative stroke order, no flourish. She uses a fountain pen by preference; the dōjō's wall scrolls are in her hand.
- **Texts and digital messages:** terse, punctuated, no emoji, no abbreviation. *"On my way."* *"Ten minutes."* *"Don't."* Voice notes essentially never; she dislikes leaving her voice in machines.
- **Email:** formal headers and salutations, paragraph structure, signed with full name. Reads like correspondence from a different decade. Replies within twenty-four hours or not at all.
- **Phone:** answers on the second ring, identifies herself by surname, ends calls without long farewells — frequently a flat *"Good"* or *"Understood"* and the line is closed.
- **Public-facing speech / press:** declines. The Daughters of the Dragon's public-facing voice is Misty; Colleen is structurally invisible to media by design.

## 10. Linguistic Tells — Summary for the File

For analysts cross-referencing audio or transcript against subject:

1. **Pre-answer nasal inhale.** Reliable across decades.
2. **First-person avoidance** via pro-drop and passive construction.
3. **"Mm"** as primary backchannel; rising in frequency under discomfort.
4. **Verb-final English** when fatigued — diagnostic of cognitive load.
5. **Honorifics deployed straight, not ironically** — diagnostic of pre-engagement threat assessment.
6. **Japanese surfacing involuntarily** — diagnostic of grief, injury, or proximity to her grandfather's memory.
7. **Numerical precision** in distance, time, count.
8. **No filler, no profanity, no pet names, no rounding.**
9. **One-sentence grief markers** followed by permanent topical silence.
10. **The conversation she does not have** is more informative than the one she does.

The composite picture: a speaker whose language is **a smaller, sharper instance of the same discipline that organizes her body** — every utterance is *kata*, every silence is *ma-ai*, every refusal to elaborate is *zanshin* held past the cut. The communications profile is not a mask over the psychology; it *is* the psychology, in audible form.


## Predictive Model I — Routine & Social

# PREDICTIVE MODEL I — ROUTINE & SOCIAL

*A library of conditional behavioral forecasts: GIVEN [stimulus / situation] → EXPECT [observable response], with confidence notation where useful. Derived from the trauma-sublimation / warrior-monk / dismissive-secure profile established in prior sections. All predictions assume baseline (non-mission) conditions unless otherwise specified.*

---

## A. THE DAY ITSELF — DIURNAL & DOMESTIC

**GIVEN** the alarm hour on any non-operational morning → **EXPECT** wake between 04:50 and 05:20, no snooze, feet on floor inside ninety seconds of consciousness. The hour is grandfather-installed and survives jet lag, hangover, and grief. Confidence: very high. She does not require an alarm to wake; the alarm exists as a courtesy to whoever is sharing her space.

**GIVEN** the first twenty minutes of the day → **EXPECT** a fixed sequence: water (room temperature, not cold), bathroom, brief standing assessment of body (rolling each shoulder, testing the left wrist which has a chronic clicking from a 1970s parry, weight shifts onto each foot), then a forty-to-sixty-minute session of *suburi* and standing meditation before any food, screen, or speech. The sequence does not vary by season, mood, or who is in the apartment. Confidence: very high.

**GIVEN** the first meal → **EXPECT** small, warm, savory: rice, miso, fish or pickles, green tea. Not sweet, not Western, not large. She will eat alone even if others are present, finish in under twelve minutes, wash her own bowl by hand before leaving the kitchen. Confidence: high.

**GIVEN** an unstructured afternoon → **EXPECT** it does not stay unstructured for more than ninety minutes. She will fill the gap with weapon maintenance, paperwork for the dōjō, correspondence with students, or a long walk. Idle hands generate low-grade restlessness she does not name as such.

**GIVEN** the evening hour → **EXPECT** dinner before 19:30, lights down by 21:30, asleep by 22:30 on most nights. Late nights are reserved for work, training, or Misty; never for entertainment. She owns a television and does not watch it.

**GIVEN** a weekend day with no obligations → **EXPECT** she invents obligations. A long sword session, a deep-clean of the dōjō floor, a trip to the fishmonger in Sunset Park, a visit to her father's grave or to an elderly student. She does not lounge. The closest she comes to leisure is reading in a single chair near a window with the radio off.

---

## B. THE BODY — POSTURE, GAIT, MICRO-TELLS

**GIVEN** standing at rest → **EXPECT** weight slightly forward, feet at approximately shoulder width, one foot fractionally ahead of the other in an unconscious *hanmi*. She does not lean against walls or counters. If she does lean, she is either injured or performing casualness for a civilian's benefit.

**GIVEN** sitting → **EXPECT** spine off the chairback, sword-side hand free, the chair angled to put a wall behind her and the door in peripheral vision. In restaurants she will request or quietly maneuver toward the corner seat without commentary. If denied the geometry she wants, she absorbs it but her shoulder line tightens by a degree only Misty would catch.

**GIVEN** walking on a city street → **EXPECT** a measured 1.4 m/s pace, even on flat ground, even when late. Her stride length does not change with mood. Footfall lands midfoot, audible to her, near-silent to others. She does not check her phone while walking. She scans intersections four steps before reaching them.

**GIVEN** a sudden loud noise (backfire, dropped tray) → **EXPECT** a half-second whole-body stillness — not a flinch, the opposite of a flinch — during which her hands relocate to neutral-ready and her eyes sweep to the source and then to the nearest exit. She will resume conversation as if nothing occurred. Civilians around her will not register that she moved at all. Confidence: very high.

**GIVEN** physical contact initiated without warning by a stranger (handshake offered from the side, a clap on the shoulder) → **EXPECT** a controlled non-flinch with a quarter-step weight shift; the hand is accepted but her body has already calculated three responses she will not need. With friends she has *trained herself* to permit casual contact; with strangers, contact is tolerated, not welcomed.

**GIVEN** any room she enters → **EXPECT** an unconscious threat-inventory completed inside four seconds: exits, sightlines, improvised weapons, persons of concern, persons of vulnerability. She will not name what she has done. She will know, three hours later, the color of the busboy's apron.

**GIVEN** the resettling of her hand near her hip or near a saya → **EXPECT** the conversation is approximately one sentence from resolution, in one direction or another. This is the single most reliable escalation tell in her behavioral repertoire.

---

## C. SPEECH, LANGUAGE, COMMUNICATION

**GIVEN** any greeting → **EXPECT** her name spoken once, a small nod, eye contact held for a beat longer than American convention but shorter than confrontation. No "how are you," no weather. With Japanese-speaking elders the bow deepens by a precise increment; with students it shortens; with Misty there is no greeting at all, only continuation.

**GIVEN** a question she finds intrusive → **EXPECT** a pause of one to two seconds, then a true but minimal answer, then a redirect to the questioner. She does not lie to deflect; she trims. People often leave conversations with her feeling listened to and realize hours later she told them nothing.

**GIVEN** small talk at a party or social obligation → **EXPECT** she finds a single person to speak with and stays with them until a graceful exit presents. She does not circulate. If forced to circulate (a dōjō fundraiser, an honoring of her father's academic work), she does it on a clock, in a sequence, like a kata.

**GIVEN** voicemail → **EXPECT** her own outgoing message is six seconds long, last name only. Her returned calls happen within twenty-four hours, typically in the evening, from a landline when one is available. She prefers text to call and call to email and email to any social platform, which she does not use.

**GIVEN** written correspondence → **EXPECT** short, declarative, signed *C. Wing* in fountain pen for personal notes and printed for business. Birthday cards to students are handwritten; she remembers every birthday in the dōjō roster without a reminder system.

**GIVEN** a compliment → **EXPECT** a nod, possibly "thank you," no deflection and no inflation. She does not return the compliment reflexively. She receives praise the way she receives a kata correction: noted, integrated, not dwelt upon.

**GIVEN** a request to talk about her feelings → **EXPECT** a slow blink, a reframe into action ("what do you want to do about it?"), and if pressed, a sentence so concise it functions as a closed door. The avoidant tilt is not hostile; it is a structural limit.

---

## D. THE MISTY DYAD

**GIVEN** Misty arriving unannounced → **EXPECT** zero surprise registered. A drawer opens for the second mug. The kettle goes on without comment. They can sit in the same room for an hour exchanging fewer than thirty words and consider it a satisfactory visit.

**GIVEN** a disagreement with Misty about an operation → **EXPECT** Colleen states her position once, fully, without volume; listens to Misty's counter without interruption; concedes if persuaded, holds if not. They do not relitigate. If they cannot reconcile, they split tasks and reconvene at result.

**GIVEN** Misty injured → **EXPECT** Colleen at the hospital within the hour, silent, in the chair nearest the door, leaving only to bring food Misty actually likes (not flowers, not cards). She will not cry where Misty can see her. She may not cry at all; the affect routes into a training session at 02:00.

**GIVEN** a third party speaking dismissively of Misty in Colleen's hearing → **EXPECT** one warning, quiet, with eye contact. There is no second warning.

**GIVEN** Misty's birthday → **EXPECT** something handmade or hand-selected, never wrapped showily — a knife sharpened to specification, a bottle of something specific, a meal cooked at the apartment. Affection is delivered as utility.

**GIVEN** prolonged separation from Misty (months) → **EXPECT** weekly check-in, three minutes, ostensibly about logistics, secretly about presence. Colleen will not name the function of the call. Neither will Misty.

---

## E. DANIEL RAND & ROMANTIC REGISTER

**GIVEN** Danny departing for K'un-Lun on no notice → **EXPECT** she helps him pack, sees him to the door, returns to whatever she was doing within ten minutes. No scene, no extended embrace, no asking when he'll return. The composure is real and it is also a mechanism.

**GIVEN** Danny's return after months away → **EXPECT** a meal, a night together, and a resumption of routine inside seventy-two hours. The relationship's reset latency is short because it was never deep enough to require rebuilding. This is a feature for both of them.

**GIVEN** a new attraction (man or woman — the record does not foreclose) → **EXPECT** long latency before any action; observation, slow assessment, preference for someone whose life will not require her to surrender solitude. She does not flirt in a verbal register. Interest is signaled by *making time*, which from her is a substantial gift.

**GIVEN** a partner attempting to escalate emotional intimacy through verbal disclosure → **EXPECT** receptivity to the disclosure, very little reciprocal disclosure, and an eventual offer of presence-instead-of-words — sitting close, training together, cooking. Partners who can read this thrive with her; partners who require throughput leave.

**GIVEN** sexual context → **EXPECT** the same disciplined embodiment present elsewhere — attentive, unhurried, not performative, not verbose. She does not narrate.

---

## F. STUDENTS AND THE DŌJŌ

**GIVEN** a new student's first class → **EXPECT** thirty minutes of footwork and posture, no weapon contact, an evaluation Colleen has completed inside ninety seconds and will not share. She remembers their name from intake. She remembers their bow angle from week three.

**GIVEN** a student making a sloppy cut → **EXPECT** correction by physical adjustment of the student's hands, hips, blade angle — not by lecture. One sentence of explanation, if any. She does not embarrass students in front of the class; private corrections happen at the door after.

**GIVEN** a student crying in the dōjō → **EXPECT** the class continues without comment; she will find the student afterward, hand them water, sit with them for as long as they need, ask one question, and listen. She does not hug unless hugged first.

**GIVEN** a student of color, particularly a young woman, particularly one with trauma history → **EXPECT** an unspoken extra-attentiveness; longer eye contact during corrections, occasional waived fees handled invisibly through the books, an invitation to the smaller advanced sessions earlier than seniority would dictate. The selection is not announced; the student notices a year in.

**GIVEN** a male student displaying disrespect toward a female student → **EXPECT** the male student is sparred with personally by Colleen the following session, in a way that is technically instructive and physically humiliating, after which the lesson is considered delivered. He either adjusts or leaves. She does not explain the sparring.

**GIVEN** a Daughters of the Dragon recruit during operational training → **EXPECT** higher demand, less warmth, more endurance load — the recruit is being prepared for a life Colleen knows the cost of. The warmth arrives only after the recruit has earned the right to be worried about.

---

## G. FAMILY OF ORIGIN, HERITAGE, MEMORY

**GIVEN** her father's death anniversary → **EXPECT** a visit to the grave, a stop at his old Columbia office building (now occupied by strangers; she stands across the street), and a longer evening kata than usual. She will not speak of him that day. She may speak of him a week later, obliquely, to Misty.

**GIVEN** her grandfather's photograph or named invocation → **EXPECT** the smallest possible facial change — softening at the corners of the mouth, a nod that is also a bow. He remains the loudest internal voice and she does not pretend otherwise.

**GIVEN** an interaction with an older Japanese man of grandfather's generation and bearing → **EXPECT** an unconscious deference she does not extend to anyone else — bow first, speak last, accept tea before declining anything else. The transferential pull is strong and she knows it.

**GIVEN** the question "are you American or Japanese" from a stranger → **EXPECT** a flat, courteous "yes," with no smile, and a change of subject. From a friend, a longer answer that still does not resolve the question, because the question does not resolve.

**GIVEN** racialized harassment on the street (anti-Asian, common in her city, escalated post-2020 in any modernized reading) → **EXPECT** de-escalation attempted first, eye contact held, voice low. If physical contact is initiated, the response is proportional, decisive, and over inside two seconds. She does not file reports. She does not post about it. She tells Misty.

**GIVEN** an invitation to speak on a panel about Asian American identity or representation → **EXPECT** polite decline. She does not believe her life is a thesis.

---

## H. MONEY, OBJECTS, CONSUMPTION

**GIVEN** her finances → **EXPECT** modest, organized, conservatively invested, with a disproportionate cash reserve held physically in two locations she has not told anyone about. She does not carry debt. The dōjō runs lean and clean; books reconciled monthly by her own hand.

**GIVEN** a major purchase decision → **EXPECT** long latency, comparison against function not brand, preference for objects that will last decades. Her kitchen knives are older than most of her students. Her boots are resoled, not replaced.

**GIVEN** a gift of luxury (a bottle of expensive scotch, a designer item from a grateful client) → **EXPECT** gracious acceptance, then re-gifting to someone who will use it. She keeps the card.

**GIVEN** her wardrobe → **EXPECT** a tight palette (black, charcoal, indigo, cream, occasional deep red), natural fibers, repeating silhouettes, nothing that restricts a draw. She owns one formal outfit and it has lasted twelve years.

**GIVEN** a new piece of technology → **EXPECT** late adoption, minimum competence acquired efficiently once committed, no curiosity beyond function. She uses her phone as phone, map, and camera; she does not scroll.

---

## I. FOOD, DRINK, SENSORY

**GIVEN** a choice of restaurant → **EXPECT** small, family-run, Japanese or Sichuan or Korean, knows the owner, sits where she sits. She tips well. She does not photograph food.

**GIVEN** an offer of alcohol → **EXPECT** accepts sake or whisky in social contexts, one or two pours, never to intoxication. She has not been visibly drunk in adult life that the record can confirm; she will not be. Loss of control is non-negotiable.

**GIVEN** coffee versus tea → **EXPECT** tea by overwhelming default — sencha in the morning, hojicha in the evening, genmaicha when grading. She drinks coffee only in operational settings where it functions as a tool.

**GIVEN** sweet foods → **EXPECT** rare interest, occasional acceptance of *wagashi* with tea, no chocolate habit, no dessert order.

**GIVEN** music in her own space → **EXPECT** silence preferred; if music, instrumental, often *shakuhachi* or classical strings, low volume, never lyrics in English during meditation. In Misty's car she tolerates whatever Misty has on without comment.

---

## J. TECHNOLOGY, MEDIA, INFORMATION

**GIVEN** the news cycle → **EXPECT** a brief morning skim of one paper (print preferred), a check on weather and headlines, no further consumption. She does not doomscroll. She does not have opinions ready for new outrages; she develops them slowly or not at all.

**GIVEN** social media → **EXPECT** no personal presence. The dōjō has a minimal website with class times and a contact form. She has resisted being photographed for it.

**GIVEN** a journalist or podcaster reaching out → **EXPECT** no reply on first contact; a polite, brief decline on second; nothing on third. She is not building a brand.

**GIVEN** surveillance awareness in modern urban environment → **EXPECT** baseline assumption that cameras exist and are recording, behavior calibrated accordingly without paranoia. She varies routes mildly, not theatrically. She uses cash often. She does not photograph identifying details of students.

---

## K. RITUAL, RELIGION, MEANING

**GIVEN** the question of belief → **EXPECT** an answer that locates her in practice rather than doctrine — bushidō as ethics, Zen aesthetic, ancestral observance at the home shrine she maintains for her mother and grandfather. She is not a churchgoer of any tradition. She is not a non-believer.

**GIVEN** a death in her circle → **EXPECT** she handles logistics — calls, transportation, food deliveries for the bereaved — and grieves through movement. She will visit graves on solar anniversaries. She lights incense on the shrine for new losses on the night she learns of them.

**GIVEN** New Year (Western) → **EXPECT** quiet, early bed. **GIVEN** Shōgatsu → **EXPECT** observed: ozōni, the home cleaned beforehand, the shrine attended, Misty invited and Misty almost always present.

**GIVEN** her own birthday → **EXPECT** a longer training session, a meal with Misty, no party, no announcement.

---

## L. CIVIC LIFE, AUTHORITY, INSTITUTIONS

**GIVEN** an encounter with NYPD → **EXPECT** courtesy without warmth, minimal answers, knowledge of her rights deployed quietly, an attorney's number memorized. She does not trust the institution; she does not provoke it. With individual officers (Misty's old precinct ties) she is correct and reserved.

**GIVEN** jury duty → **EXPECT** she serves. She would be an unusually careful juror, attentive, quiet in deliberations until a precise late intervention.

**GIVEN** voting → **EXPECT** consistent local participation, less interest in spectacle elections, supports candidates who fund community programs over carceral expansion. She does not display signage.

**GIVEN** a request to consult for federal agencies (FBI, DHS) on Asian organized crime → **EXPECT** declined. She has watched institutions weaponize community knowledge before. Misty's old NYPD contacts she answers selectively; federal asks she does not.

---

## M. SLEEP, SOLITUDE, INTERIOR

**GIVEN** the hour before sleep → **EXPECT** sword cleaned and racked, kitchen wiped, brief seated meditation, a chapter of something old (history, poetry, sword treatise) in a hard chair, never in bed. Bed is for sleep.

**GIVEN** dreams → **EXPECT** unreported, not because absent but because not the kind of material she narrates. If pressed, she might admit to recurring training-floor dreams in which her grandfather corrects her stance.

**GIVEN** a night she cannot sleep → **EXPECT** she rises rather than fights it, trains for forty minutes, returns to bed. She does not take sleep aids; she does not drink to sleep.

**GIVEN** solitude of a day or two → **EXPECT** restored, not depleted. She refills here. **GIVEN** solitude of a week or more without contact with Misty → **EXPECT** an unprompted call placed by Colleen, framed as logistical.

---

## N. EDGE CASES — SOCIAL MISFIRES THE CANON DID NOT SHOW

**GIVEN** an aggressive drunk on the subway harassing another passenger → **EXPECT** she positions her body between aggressor and target without speech, makes eye contact with the aggressor, and waits. The situation resolves through his recalibration nine times in ten. The tenth time it resolves more quickly.

**GIVEN** a child lost in a public space → **EXPECT** she kneels to the child's height, speaks low and slowly, locates an authority figure she has assessed as safe, stays until handoff is complete. She is unexpectedly good with children, who read her stillness as trustworthy.

**GIVEN** a panhandler → **EXPECT** small bills given without speech or commentary, more often than her income would predict, never to the same person on consecutive days (a calibrated practice, not sentiment).

**GIVEN** being recognized publicly by a former student years later → **EXPECT** instant recall of name, posture corrected in the student in the same gesture as the greeting, three minutes of attention, a graceful close.

**GIVEN** an invitation to her own surprise party → **EXPECT** she has known about it for two weeks and arrives anyway, acts surprised competently, leaves at a reasonable hour, thanks the host personally the next day. The performance is a courtesy; she does not mistake it for joy.

**GIVEN** a wedding → **EXPECT** attended if Misty; conditional otherwise. She does not dance. She will hold someone's drink, someone's child, someone's coat.

**GIVEN** a funeral → **EXPECT** present, early, in the back, in dark colors, staying through the reception only as long as needed to deliver food to the family.

---

## O. THE LONG TELLS

Across decades the following will hold, regardless of era or modernization:

- She will not be late to anything important. Ever.
- She will not raise her voice in anger. The few times she has, those present remember the year.
- She will outlive most of her grudges by outlasting them; she does not pursue revenge as project, though she will close a loop if it crosses her threshold.
- She will be, at sixty and at seventy and at eighty, on the dōjō floor at dawn.
- She will die with her affairs in order, her sword cleaned, the books reconciled, a note for Misty in the top drawer of the desk, and not a single thing on social media to outlive her.

These predictions form the substrate against which any deviation — a slept-through alarm, a raised voice, a late arrival, an unsolicited disclosure — should be read as significant signal rather than noise. The steadiness is the baseline. The crack in the steadiness is the data.


## Predictive Model II — Crisis, Betrayal & the Wound

# PREDICTIVE MODEL II — CRISIS, BETRAYAL & THE WOUND

*Conditional behavioral forecasts under acute stress, threat-to-kin, moral compromise, and direct contact with the unprocessed material. Read as: GIVEN [stimulus], EXPECT [response with specificity], CONFIDENCE [low/moderate/high], TELL [observable marker], DECOMPENSATION VECTOR [if applicable].*

---

## 6.1 BASELINE CRISIS RESPONSE — THE STILLNESS CURVE

The single most reliable forecast in this file: under acute threat, Colleen Wing's affect, language, and movement compress rather than expand. The error civilians and most operators make is reading the compression as calm. It is not calm. It is the kata-before-cut state — a regulated pre-violence posture in which her parasympathetic and sympathetic systems are both running hot, mediated by three decades of trained breath control. The face goes neutral; the shoulders drop a quarter inch; the dominant hand stops gesturing and seeks the saya, a hip, the back of a chair, or — absent any of these — comes to rest palm-down on the thigh with thumb under the index finger in a grip-prep configuration.

**GIVEN** an unexpected armed entry into a room she occupies, **EXPECT** her to (1) exhale fully before the door is half-open, (2) reposition her hips so the dominant-side leg loads, (3) speak first if a verbal off-ramp exists, with the lowest sentence-count and lowest pitch she has used all day, (4) refuse to raise her hands in surrender posture until tactically optimal — Japanese-sword-trained operators do not signal compliance through the upper body because the upper body is the weapon delivery system. **CONFIDENCE: high.** **TELL:** the pre-cut exhale; the dropped shoulders; the dead-quiet diaphragm.

**GIVEN** escalation beyond the verbal off-ramp, **EXPECT** decision latency under 400ms once she has committed. The bushidō rule-set she runs under pressure is *not* deliberative; it is pre-loaded. Once she decides to cut, she does not stop mid-motion to re-evaluate. The civilian/SHIELD-trained instinct to call "stand down" mid-engagement will not be honored. **DECOMPENSATION VECTOR:** committed-cut momentum, see §6.7.

**GIVEN** crisis duration exceeding her acute window (~45 minutes of continuous engagement), **EXPECT** a second-order compression: she stops eating, stops drinking, stops speaking except for tactical instruction, and her micro-expressions cease entirely. Operators around her will read this as cold and may assume she has disengaged emotionally. She has not. She is running a longer kata.

---

## 6.2 THREAT-TO-MISTY — THE COLLAPSE OF STRATEGIC PATIENCE

This is the single largest pressure-coordinate in the dossier and the predictions here are the highest-confidence in the document.

**GIVEN** credible intelligence that Misty Knight has been taken, wounded, or targeted, **EXPECT** Colleen to abandon ongoing operations within the hour, including operations she has personally vouched for and operations involving third-party lives. This is not negotiable behavior; it is identity-level. **CONFIDENCE: very high.** **TELL:** she will not announce the abandonment; she will simply be gone. Equipment retrieved from the dōjō office safe (the wakizashi she does not carry publicly; a secondary medical kit; cash in three currencies; one burner) within seven to nine minutes of receiving the call.

**GIVEN** that the threat to Misty is from an actor she has previously broken bread with, **EXPECT** zero hesitation derived from prior relationship. Bushidō does not weight social debt against an attack on chosen kin. Old allies who move against Misty receive the same response as strangers, delivered with the additional courtesy of being told why before the cut, if time permits.

**GIVEN** that Misty has been killed, **EXPECT** — and this is the prediction with the gravest operational implications — the bushidō container to hold for roughly 72 hours of tactical pursuit, then to crack. The crack will not present as grief in any legible form. It will present as a methodical, sleepless, eat-standing-up campaign against every node connected to the killing, conducted without backup, without sleep deeper than 90 minutes, and without the consultative humility she normally extends to Danny or to the Daughters. The honor-bound overcommitment vector (§6.7) becomes the operating mode rather than the failure mode. Decompensation here looks like *function*, not breakdown — which is what makes it dangerous.

**GIVEN** that she is forced to choose between rescuing Misty and honoring a prior commitment to a third party (student, client, Danny), **EXPECT** Misty to win. The bushidō-trained reader will expect honor of contract to compete; in Colleen's case the contract-with-Misty is the deepest contract she has ever signed and predates every other operational vow. She will execute the choice cleanly and accept the moral debt to the abandoned third party without flinching. She will pay that debt later, in full, and without complaint.

---

## 6.3 BODILY SOVEREIGNTY THREATS — THE FOURTH INVASION SCENARIO

The dossier flags three prior canonical bodily invasions (trafficking-attempt drugging; Kara-Kai conditioning; vampiric transformation). The sublimation defense has absorbed all three. The forecast here is for the fourth.

**GIVEN** any chemical agent, telepathic intrusion, magical compulsion, or pheromone-class influence applied to her person, **EXPECT** an immediate, disproportionate, almost feral resistance phase — far in excess of what the tactical situation requires. She will accept lethal-grade injury rather than allow a needle to land. **CONFIDENCE: very high.** This is not assessed risk-calculus; this is the sublimation defense activating to preserve itself. The cost of a fourth successful invasion is not tactical; it is the dissolution of the central self-organizing premise of her adult life (the disciplined body as the one thing she owns), and her organism appears to know this.

**GIVEN** an invasion is successful nonetheless, **EXPECT** — in the immediate aftermath — a withdrawal of 48 to 96 hours from all human contact, conducted in the dōjō with the doors barred, during which she will run her grandfather's full kata sequence to exhaustion, sleep three hours, and run it again. No one is to enter. Danny will be turned away. Misty will be granted a five-minute audience at the door and no more. The somatic re-occupation of the body is the only reset protocol she has.

**GIVEN** a fourth invasion occurs while she is operationally committed to protect another party, **EXPECT** the sublimation to fail catastrophically. The container is sized for trauma metabolized over time, not stacked acute insults. The failure mode here is the one scenario where she may genuinely break — not into incompetence, but into a months-long fugue of unsanctioned, off-the-books killing of every actor associated with the invasion, conducted with bushidō rationalization but in fact driven by the un-metabolizable rage the defense was built to prevent her ever feeling. **DECOMPENSATION VECTOR: maximum.** This is the failure she cannot pre-empt.

---

## 6.4 MORAL INJURY — BEING MADE TO VIOLATE HER CODE WHILE BELIEVING SHE UPHOLDS IT

The Kara-Kai episode is the template. The forecast governs any recurrence of the structural pattern: deception that routes her honor against her own values.

**GIVEN** post-hoc discovery that she has acted on falsified intelligence and consequently harmed an innocent or an ally, **EXPECT** an immediate cessation of active operations and a private accounting phase. She will not seek absolution from Danny, Misty, or a confessor; she will seek the harmed party (or their kin) and present herself unarmed for whatever they wish to extract. **CONFIDENCE: high.** This is a samurai-retainer's accounting protocol, not a therapeutic one. She is not asking forgiveness; she is offering balance.

**GIVEN** the harmed party demands her life, **EXPECT** her to consider the demand seriously and at length. She will not comply — Misty and the dōjō hold her on the side of continued existence — but she will not dismiss the demand, and she will carry the unpaid debt as a weight that visibly shortens her speech for months afterward. **TELL:** she stops drinking even social sake; cuts coffee; eats less; and the kata sessions lengthen by roughly thirty percent.

**GIVEN** the deception originated from an institutional actor she trusted (Avengers-tier, government, a peer dōjō), **EXPECT** permanent severance from that institution — not loud, not announced, simply absent. She does not maintain relationships with sources of moral compromise. **CONFIDENCE: high.**

**GIVEN** repeated moral injuries within a short window (two or more inside a year), **EXPECT** her to consider returning to Honshu for a sustained period — six months minimum — to re-anchor in the source-discipline. This is her one-way valve. It has not yet been deployed in canon at length; the prediction is that it will be deployed eventually under sufficient accumulated weight.

---

## 6.5 THE AMERICAN/JAPANESE SEAM — IDENTITY-LEVEL PROVOCATION

The seam is the unexamined fault line. Most provocations along it land softly because most provocateurs are clumsy and she is practiced at not answering.

**GIVEN** a sophisticated antagonist who frames the choice as "which half are you really," **EXPECT** her to deflect verbally with a one-line acknowledgment and a tactical pivot. **TELL:** a microscopic delay (~200–400ms) before the deflection — the only place in her operational presentation where a pause appears that is not strategic. The pause is the wound.

**GIVEN** the antagonist persists and ties the question to action (forcing her to choose between an American institutional loyalty and a Japanese traditional one, e.g., between NYPD/SHIELD protocol and a sensei's instruction), **EXPECT** her to choose the Japanese-traditional side approximately 70% of the time, with the percentage rising sharply if the American institution has previously failed her. **CONFIDENCE: moderate-high.** The deeper attachment figure is her grandfather; the deeper code is bushidō; the deeper kin-system is the dōjō lineage. America raised her father and let him be remote; Japan raised her.

**GIVEN** the antagonist is himself Japanese and frames her as insufficiently Japanese — half-blood, diaspora, gaijin-trained — **EXPECT** the deepest wound this dossier predicts short of Misty's death. She will not show it. She will become more formal in posture, switch to keigo register if Japanese is being spoken, and execute the operational answer with extreme prejudice. The provocateur will rarely live to refine the insult. **TELL:** the formality itself; an unexplained reach for an older sword if one is available.

---

## 6.6 BETRAYAL — THE DANNY VECTOR, THE MISTY VECTOR, THE STUDENT VECTOR

Different betrayals route through different containers.

**GIVEN** betrayal by Daniel Rand — infidelity, deception about K'un-Lun matters, alignment with a faction she opposes — **EXPECT** a quiet, complete relational reset. She will not perform anger. The relationship will simply move from romantic-affectionate to professional-courteous within a week, and she will deny him no operational support he requests but will share no further interior life. **CONFIDENCE: high.** The avoidant-attachment substrate makes this exit clean; the romance with Danny has always been structured for survivable disengagement.

**GIVEN** betrayal by Misty Knight — and the dossier should be explicit that this is the scenario with the highest emotional stakes she has never been forced to face — **EXPECT** a months-long inability to operate at full coordination, the only predicted scenario in which her professional competence is degraded by an interpersonal event. She will not retaliate. She will not speak of it. She will reduce contact to operational minimum and grieve the relationship as if Misty had died, because in her psychic economy the chosen-sister Misty has died. **CONFIDENCE: moderate-high** (extrapolated; not directly tested in canon). **DECOMPENSATION VECTOR:** the sublimation defense relies on Misty as a load-bearing wall; remove the wall and the architecture is compromised.

**GIVEN** betrayal by a student — a Daughter of the Dragon recruit turning to the other side, accepting money to compromise the dōjō, harming a fellow trainee — **EXPECT** a teacher's response, not an enemy's. She will pursue the student personally, attempt to recover them once, and on refusal, execute the necessary outcome with the gravity of a master who has failed a transmission. The grief she will not show for the relationship she will show in the increased severity of her teaching for the next generation.

**GIVEN** betrayal by a former lover other than Danny (the record is thin here but the pattern is inferable), **EXPECT** clean severance with no further audience granted. She does not relitigate.

---

## 6.7 HONOR-BOUND OVERCOMMITMENT — THE COMMITTED-CUT MOMENTUM

The single most operationally dangerous feature of her decision architecture. Once the cut is committed, she does not retract; the bushidō frame retroactively justifies the lethal force as honorable rather than reconsidered.

**GIVEN** new information arriving mid-engagement that would cause a non-samurai-trained operator to pull the cut, **EXPECT** Colleen to complete the motion approximately 80% of the time. The 20% retraction window requires either (a) Misty intervening physically or verbally, (b) a child appearing in the line, or (c) Danny invoking K'un-Lun-grade moral authority she recognizes. **CONFIDENCE: high.** **TELL:** there is no tell; the cut completes faster than the recognition.

**GIVEN** post-cut realization that the cut was wrong, see §6.4 (moral injury protocol).

**GIVEN** a sequence of three or more committed-cut engagements inside a 90-day window, **EXPECT** an unannounced personal retreat from operations — she will recognize, without articulating it, that her rule-set is running too hot and that she needs to re-anchor. The retreat will be framed publicly as a teaching commitment or a personal trip; the actual purpose is recalibration.

---

## 6.8 TEMPTATION — WHAT SHE WILL AND WILL NOT BE BOUGHT BY

**GIVEN** financial inducement of any magnitude, **EXPECT** refusal. She has lived on dōjō income and Nightwing/Daughters fees for decades; money is not a lever. **CONFIDENCE: very high.**

**GIVEN** offered status — a seat on an Avengers-tier roster, a sanctioned-team affiliation, a State Department consultancy — **EXPECT** polite refusal. Institutional embedding violates the small-accountable-units worldview and would route her honor through a chain of command she cannot vet. **CONFIDENCE: high.**

**GIVEN** offered access to her grandfather's archive, lost kata, or a sword of historical provenance tied to Kenji Ozawa's lineage, **EXPECT** genuine temptation and a careful, multi-step verification of the offer's legitimacy. This is one of two known levers. **CONFIDENCE: moderate-high.** The provenance lever can route her into compromising positions before she recognizes the route.

**GIVEN** offered the chance to undo the Kara-Kai episode — magical, temporal, or memory-altering — **EXPECT** refusal, but a refusal that costs her something visible. She will not unmake the wound because the wound is now part of the discipline. The refusal itself is the second-strongest evidence in this file of the depth of the integration. **CONFIDENCE: moderate.**

**GIVEN** offered the chance to save Misty at the cost of her own honor (commit a dishonorable act and Misty lives), **EXPECT** her to commit the act and pay the honor cost without negotiation. Bushidō ranks kin-protection above abstract code-purity when the two collide, and Misty is the kin. **CONFIDENCE: high.** **DECOMPENSATION VECTOR:** the surviving Colleen post-trade will require years of recalibration and may permanently retire the public Nightwing identity.

---

## 6.9 INTERROGATION & CAPTIVITY

**GIVEN** capture by a competent adversary, **EXPECT** no information disclosed under standard duress. She has been conditioned by Kara-Kai once and will not surrender volition again at a verbal level. **TELL:** she will sit in seiza if floor-permitted, eyes half-lowered, and breathe.

**GIVEN** prolonged captivity (>96 hours), **EXPECT** her to begin a covert isometric and breath-regulation regimen invisible to most observers — micro-tension cycles maintaining muscle integrity, paced breathing maintaining cardiovascular tone. She will be operational at 85% within 30 seconds of restraint removal.

**GIVEN** the adversary offers chemical interrogation, see §6.3.

**GIVEN** the adversary threatens Misty/Danny/students to extract compliance, **EXPECT** her to comply tactically while planning the adversary's death. The compliance will be exact, calm, and convincing. The death will arrive later, at the time of her choosing, and will not be telegraphed.

---

## 6.10 DANIEL'S PERMANENT LOSS — THE UNMODELED SCENARIO

Danny has died and returned often enough that her psychic economy treats his death as recoverable. The forecast for genuine, irreversible loss is therefore the least-evidence-supported and most speculative in this section.

**GIVEN** Danny dies in a manner she recognizes as final (mystic verification, K'un-Lun confirmation, no resurrection vector), **EXPECT** a delayed grief response — weeks of operational normalcy followed by an abrupt withdrawal once the absence becomes structural rather than situational. **CONFIDENCE: moderate.** She will not have rehearsed this loss the way she has half-rehearsed Misty's.

**GIVEN** stewardship of the Rand legacy infrastructure falls to her, **EXPECT** acceptance without flinch and execution to a high standard. The vocational container will absorb the grief; see the general sublimation pattern.

**GIVEN** a K'un-Lun successor to Danny appears and requires training, **EXPECT** her to undertake it. Lineage transmission is a recognized obligation in her code.

---

## 6.11 THE DECOMPENSATION HIERARCHY — RANKED

For analyst convenience, the decompensation vectors in ascending order of severity:

1. **Three-cut-window overcommitment** (§6.7) — self-correcting via retreat.
2. **Single moral injury via deception** (§6.4) — metabolized over months via accounting protocol.
3. **Daniel's permanent death** (§6.10) — speculative; vocationally absorbable.
4. **Betrayal by Danny** (§6.6) — clean relational reset; no operational degradation.
5. **Fourth bodily invasion, isolated** (§6.3) — 48-96 hour somatic re-occupation; recoverable.
6. **American/Japanese seam, weaponized by sophisticated antagonist** (§6.5) — wounds beneath the operational layer.
7. **Misty killed** (§6.2) — 72-hour container then function-as-decompensation; sleepless campaign.
8. **Misty betrays her** (§6.6) — load-bearing wall removed; months of degraded coordination.
9. **Fourth bodily invasion stacked with active protection commitment** (§6.3) — sublimation catastrophic failure; off-the-books killing fugue.
10. **Forced trade of honor for Misty's life** (§6.8) — public identity retirement; years of recalibration; survives but is not the same operator after.

The pattern across the hierarchy: the wounds that touch the body are recoverable; the wounds that touch the chosen-kin architecture are not. This is the inversion of what her bushidō presentation suggests and the single most important analytic conclusion to carry into the synthesis stage. **She does not break when you cut her. She breaks when you reach Misty.**


## Vulnerabilities & Leverage Compendium

# VULNERABILITIES & LEVERAGE COMPENDIUM: COLLEEN WING

*Compiled for understanding and protection. This section maps every documented and inferred lever — the places where the subject can be reached, calmed, persuaded, provoked, predicted, or destabilized. The compendium is exhaustive by design; in a protective frame, knowing every door is the prerequisite to closing them before adversaries find them.*

---

## I. THE ARCHITECTURE OF HER VULNERABILITY

Before enumerating individual levers, the structural picture: Wing's psyche is not fragile but it is **load-bearing in a particular way**. Her stability rests on a small number of containers — the sword, the dōjō, the partnership with Misty Knight, the bushidō frame, the body she has trained for forty years — and each container holds material that would otherwise spill catastrophically. A clinician or adversary who understood this would not attack her directly; they would attack a container. Punching her does nothing. Removing her sword, her partner, her students, or her bodily sovereignty does everything.

This is the inversion that defines her threat surface: **she is hardest to break where most people are softest (direct confrontation, intimidation, physical pain, public humiliation) and softest where most people are hardest (the integrity of her chosen frame, the inviolability of her honor, the safety of two or three specific people, the sovereignty of her own body).**

What follows is the full map.

---

## II. PRIMARY PRESSURE POINTS — RANKED BY YIELD

### 1. Mercedes "Misty" Knight

The single highest-leverage coordinate in her life. Not Daniel Rand. Not her father. Not her grandfather's memory. Misty.

- **Credible threat to Misty's life or freedom** collapses strategic patience within seconds. The composure does not break upward into rage — it compresses downward into immediate, often unilateral, action. She will leave a hospital bed. She will violate a standing agreement. She will accept a tactically losing engagement if the alternative is delay.
- **Threat to Misty by Wing's own hand** — the Kara-Kai signature — is the maximum-pain coordinate. Any scenario that positions her as the instrument of Misty's harm (mind control, deception, mistaken identity, coerced choice between Misty and a student) reaches a region of her psyche that her ritual defenses do not cover. This is the one wound the kata cannot contain.
- **Misty's disapproval** is the only social sanction that registers fully. Danny's disappointment she can tolerate; a student's she can correct; Misty's silence after a disagreement reorganizes her week.
- *Protective implication.* Adversaries who study her will identify Misty within hours of opening a file. Any protection plan must treat the two as a single attack surface. Separating them for "safety" is the worst possible move — it removes both her primary regulator and her primary motivation to remain measured.

### 2. Bodily Sovereignty

Three documented invasions — the trafficker's drugs in *Marvel Premiere* #20, the Kara-Kai conditioning, the vampiric transformation in the late Claremont run. The pattern is the most psychologically loaded fact in her file and the writers have never let her speak to it.

- **Any chemical, hypnotic, telepathic, or mystical override** reaches a substrate her sublimation defenses do not protect. A fourth invasion would likely puncture the structure in a way the prior three did not, because the redundancy itself would prove that her training cannot make her body hers.
- **Needles, restraints, anesthesia, sedation** — even consensual medical contexts trigger micro-resistance. Watch for her negotiating to remain conscious during procedures, asking for local rather than general, declining post-op opioids, refusing benzodiazepines for anything.
- **Touch without warning** from behind or from above. Not panicked, but corrected — the hand is moved or the angle is broken before conscious thought.
- *Protective implication.* Telepaths, chemists, and mystics are her structural counters. Any protective detail around her should include psychic shielding and a trusted, pre-approved medical contact she has personally vetted.

### 3. Dishonor by Deception

The failure mode she cannot pre-empt: being made to violate her own code while believing she is upholding it. This is moral injury, not trauma in the PTSD sense, and the distinction matters because it cannot be resolved by safety; it can only be resolved by **truth, witness, and corrective action**, none of which an adversary will provide.

- Manipulating her into killing a target who turns out to be innocent, or sparing one who turns out to be a predator, attacks the only self-image she has built.
- False-flag operations — using her sword's reputation to commit acts she did not commit — are particularly potent because they invert the bushidō frame against her: the discipline that was supposed to make her accountable is repurposed to make her infamous.
- *Protective implication.* Information hygiene around her operations is not paranoia; it is medical care. Verify targets twice. Confirm provenance of jobs. The friend who keeps her from being deceived is doing more for her than the friend who keeps her from being shot.

### 4. The American/Japanese Seam

Her entire life is the architecture of not having to answer the question. Lee Wing's Columbia office and Kenji Ozawa's mountain dōjō do not reconcile; she has organized her existence so that the seam is structural rather than confrontational.

- Identity challenges framed as **"which are you really"** — by relatives, journalists, ideologues, or enemies trying to wound — land harder than her face shows. She does not rebut them; she goes still and changes the subject. The stillness is the tell.
- Encounters with the Japanese-American community where she is positioned as either insufficiently Japanese or performatively so produce a low, persistent discomfort she will not name.
- Encounters with Japan itself (travel, family business, the maternal grandfather's surviving acquaintances) produce a regression toward greater formality and reduced English — a protective costume.
- *Protective implication.* This is a region where she does not want help and will not accept it. The respectful move is to never force the seam into language. Allies who let her be both without comment are deeply restful to her.

### 5. Daniel Rand's Eventual Permanent Loss

Danny dies and returns frequently enough that she has built tolerance — a tolerance that itself becomes a vulnerability, because it has prevented her from ever fully modeling the scenario in which he does not come back.

- The relationship's tolerance for absence is mutual and has never been stress-tested by finality.
- Should Danny die permanently, she will not collapse visibly; the decompensation will be slow, six- to eighteen-month, expressed as increased solitariness, longer training sessions, reduced taking of new students, and a tightening of the Misty bond into something nearly fused.
- *Protective implication.* In the event of Danny's loss, the protective move is to insist on the dōjō remaining open, on students continuing to arrive, on Misty being physically present at intervals she does not have to request. The mistake is to leave her alone "to grieve in her own way." Her own way is the way that ends with her in the mountains.

### 6. The Containers Themselves

The sword, the dōjō, the partnership, the body — taken individually each is robust. **Taken simultaneously, their loss is the only scenario in which her structure fails.**

- The sword alone: replaceable, but the *specific* katana that descends from Kenji Ozawa is not. Theft or destruction of the inherited blade produces a measurable behavioral shift — increased pilgrimage behavior, longer meditation, reduced humor.
- The dōjō alone: rebuildable, but the loss of the *space* (and its students) removes her primary generative outlet. Without students to teach, her ritualization turns inward and unproductive.
- The partnership alone: catastrophic, addressed above.
- The body alone: a serious injury that removes her capacity to perform kenjutsu at the level she has trained to would attack the foundation that all other containers rest on. Not "she can no longer fight" — she can adapt to that — but "she can no longer move through the form."
- *Protective implication.* Adversaries planning to break her would aim to remove two containers at once. Protection planning must monitor all four and ensure none degrade simultaneously.

---

## III. SECONDARY PRESSURE POINTS

### 7. Students Under Her Care

Once she has accepted a student into the dōjō or into Daughters of the Dragon training, the obligation is structurally similar to the Misty obligation, scaled down and broadened. She will take wounds for students she has known for six weeks.

- Harm to a student on her watch produces a guilt response disproportionate to her actual culpability and not articulated. Watch for extended solo training, declined social invitations, and a marked drop in the dry humor that is her normal baseline.
- Recruitment lures — adversaries posing as prospective students to gain proximity — would work on her once. The second attempt she would smell.

### 8. Lee Wing (Father)

The relationship is the one she has never resolved and never confronted. He is alive in canon and emotionally remote; she sees him at intervals, exchanges letters, and neither of them addresses the architecture of her childhood.

- Direct harm to him would produce a complicated grief — duty without warmth, obligation without intimacy, and shame at the absence of the latter.
- Information about him she did not know — particularly anything about her mother's death, or her grandfather's relationship with him — would land hard.
- *Protective implication.* He is not a high adversary-priority target because their public connection is muted, but a careful adversary would find him. Low-visibility protection of Lee Wing is warranted and should be invisible to Colleen, who would refuse it if offered on her behalf.

### 9. The Memory of Kenji Ozawa

Her grandfather is the foundational attachment figure and the originator of the code she lives by. He is dead in canon; the relationship lives in inherited objects, taught kata, and remembered phrasing.

- Revelations about Ozawa's Imperial-era conduct — atrocity, collaboration, anything that would retroactively contaminate the moral inheritance — would attack the source of her bushidō frame itself. This is the deepest possible attack on her self-concept and the one she has no defenses against because the defenses *are* the inheritance.
- Forgery or theft of objects, documents, or kata attributed to him produces disproportionate response.
- *Protective implication.* Provenance research on the Ozawa line should be done quietly by an ally before it is done loudly by an enemy. If there is rot in the inheritance, she should hear it from someone who loves her, not from a journalist.

### 10. The Reputation of the Sword

Her name on the street — *Colleen Wing, the sword* — is operationally useful and personally meaningful. She does not court fame; she does court a particular kind of professional respect.

- Public reframing of her as a thug, mercenary-for-hire, or instrument of someone else's agenda attacks both her honor frame and her livelihood.
- Forced public appearances, interviews, costumed-hero photo ops produce strong avoidance. She is a private operator and the privacy is part of the discipline.

---

## IV. HOW TO REACH HER

### Approach Vectors That Work

- **Through Misty.** Always. The legitimacy Misty extends is the legitimacy Colleen will provisionally extend. This is not laziness on Colleen's part; it is correct delegation of trust to her most calibrated source.
- **Through shared task.** Offering her something concrete to do — protect this person, train this group, evaluate this threat — bypasses the verbal-emotional layer she finds tiresome and reaches her at the level she actually lives on.
- **Through formal courtesy.** Bow, address her properly, observe the etiquette of the dōjō when in it. She is not impressed by the performance, but she is offended by its absence, and the offense is sticky.
- **Through silence held well.** She will sit with someone in silence for an hour and feel closer to them at the end than after an hour of conversation. Allies who can hold the silence without filling it have access most people do not.
- **Through students.** Concern for one of her students — credible, specific, not performative — is one of the fastest ways to her attention.

### Approach Vectors That Fail

- **Through Danny.** He vouches less effectively for outsiders than people expect; she does not import his trust automatically.
- **Through credentials or institutional weight.** Avengers liaison, SHIELD badge, NYPD shield — these register as warning signs rather than reassurances.
- **Through emotional disclosure.** Strangers who open with vulnerability to manufacture intimacy read as either manipulative or weak. Both register as do-not-trust.
- **Through humor of the wrong register.** She has dry humor; she finds performative jocularity grating. Adversaries doing folksy charm offensives land badly.
- **Through flattery of her skill.** She knows what her skill is. Compliments read as either obvious or transactional.

---

## V. HOW TO CALM HER

When she is escalated — and "escalated" for her means stilled, quieted, gripped on the saya, breath compressed to a four-count — the de-escalation protocol is not verbal.

- **Reduce the number of people in the room.** Crowds prevent her from completing the threat assessment she has begun. Two people present (her and the regulator) is the right number.
- **Offer her a task.** "Walk the perimeter," "check on the student," "tell me what you saw" — task assignment moves her from threat-state into operator-state.
- **Do not touch her.** Even allies. The exception is Misty, who has tactile permission Colleen extends to no one else, and who knows when to use it.
- **Speak short.** Sentences of seven words or fewer. She is not in a state to parse rhetoric.
- **Name the next step concretely.** "We leave the building. We go to the dōjō. You decide what's next." Procedure soothes her in a way reassurance does not.
- **Permit her to clean a blade.** If she requests cleaning equipment after an incident, she is regulating. The request should be granted without comment. The ritual is functional.

---

## VI. HOW TO PERSUADE HER

Persuasion of Colleen Wing is a different operation than persuasion of most subjects. She does not respond to argument; she responds to **fit with the frame**.

- **Frame the request inside her existing obligations.** "This protects a student" or "this honors a promise to Misty" routes through channels already open. "This is the right thing" — abstract moral language — routes nowhere.
- **Show your work.** She wants to see the reasoning, particularly the threat assessment. Conclusions presented without method read as either incompetent or manipulative.
- **Acknowledge the cost.** Telling her honestly what an action will cost her — time, risk, alliance with X, money — builds trust faster than minimizing the cost.
- **Let her dictate execution.** She will accept a goal she did not choose; she will not accept methods imposed by someone less competent at her trade.
- **Give her the right to say no.** Persuasion attempts that foreclose refusal trigger her resistance reflex. Persuasion attempts that explicitly preserve refusal often succeed where pressure would have failed.

---

## VII. HOW TO PROVOKE HER (AND THEREFORE WHAT TO PREVENT)

This section exists so that allies recognize the levers adversaries will reach for.

- **Insult Misty in her presence.** Threat-state within two seconds. Lethal-decision-tree opens within ten.
- **Threaten or harm a student.** Same response, slower onset, longer duration.
- **Bind, drug, or restrain her against her will.** All previous adversaries who survived doing this did so by luck. Future ones should not be counted on to have the same luck.
- **Impersonate her.** Particularly using her sword's reputation for acts of cruelty. She will hunt this and she will not stop.
- **Force her into a public-relations context she did not consent to.** Less catastrophic, but produces durable enmity.
- **Treat the dōjō as a stage.** Cameras, journalists, costumed-hero photo ops on her training floor. The space is sacred to her in a specific functional sense; profanation produces cold, prolonged distance.
- **Mock the bushidō frame.** Ideological condescension — "your samurai cosplay" — does not provoke immediate response but is logged, indexed, and remembered. People who do this discover later that she has quietly excised them from her life.
- **Take a coerced cut from her.** Maneuver her into committing to a strike she would not have chosen. Once committed she does not retract, which means the provocation works by exploiting her honor structure against her judgment.

---

## VIII. HOW TO PREDICT HER

She is one of the most predictable high-functioning operators in the file system, which is itself a vulnerability — adversaries who study her can pre-position.

- **Daily ritual.** Pre-dawn kata. Sword maintenance after any deployment. Tea at specific intervals. Sleep schedule rigidly maintained when possible.
- **Routes.** Repeats. She walks the same blocks, takes the same trains, enters the dōjō through the same door. The repetition is not unconsciousness; it is efficiency, and she counter-surveils her own routes, but the routes themselves are stable.
- **Reactions to specific stimuli.** Trafficking situations — non-negotiable intervention regardless of tactical sense. Sword work by amateurs — corrective comment whether invited or not. A student in distress — immediate redirection of her schedule. Misty late to a meeting without contact — fifteen minutes of patience, then movement.
- **Escalation signature.** Stillness, not loudness. Grip resettle on the saya. Breath shortens. Word count per sentence drops. When the sentence drops to three words, the cut is decided.
- **Decision style under pressure.** Bushidō-rule-based, decisive, irreversible. She does not change her mind mid-action; she completes the action and reassesses after.
- **Sleep.** Light, easily woken, returns to sleep quickly — a trained pattern. Disrupting her sleep over multiple nights is one of the few ways to degrade her performance, but the degradation is small and she recovers within one full sleep cycle.

---

## IX. HOW TO DESTABILIZE HER (AND THEREFORE WHAT TO HARDEN)

The destabilization scenarios listed here are written to be defended against, not executed. Each is paired with a hardening recommendation.

- **Simultaneous container removal.** The catastrophic scenario: Misty taken, dōjō burned, inherited sword stolen, body compromised — in close succession. No single one breaks her; the conjunction does. *Hardening:* redundancy in each container. Backup dōjō location. Sword stored separately from her residence. Misty's protection plan independent of Colleen's. Mystical and psychic shielding maintained as a baseline, not as a crisis response.
- **Moral framing inversion.** Convince her, over months, that her code is being used to perpetuate the disorder it was meant to oppose. This is the slow attack and the most effective one because she cannot easily distinguish legitimate moral revision from adversarial undermining. *Hardening:* sustained relationships with people whose moral judgment she trusts (Misty, a small number of others) who can serve as reality testers when her frame is challenged.
- **Inheritance contamination.** Revelations about Ozawa that retroactively poison the source of her code. *Hardening:* friendly provenance research, done now, so that anything found is found by allies first.
- **Misty replacement scenario.** An adversary who successfully positions someone as Misty's functional equivalent — partner, sister, regulator — while Misty is incapacitated. Colleen would resist consciously and accept unconsciously, and the acceptance would be a vulnerability to whatever the substitute was actually working for. *Hardening:* recognition that Misty's role is structurally singular and cannot be safely outsourced even temporarily.
- **Fourth bodily invasion.** Discussed above. The structural fact is that her sublimation defense has held through three; a fourth is the empirically unmodeled case. *Hardening:* prevent it. There is no good post-hoc protocol.
- **Forcing her to choose between Misty and a student.** A constructed dilemma where both cannot be saved and she must select. The choice itself, regardless of outcome, attacks the integrated self-concept by forcing a hierarchy she has been able to maintain implicitly without ever testing. *Hardening:* tactical doctrine that prevents the dilemma from being constructed — never let her operate in a configuration where the choice becomes possible.

---

## X. WHAT SHE CANNOT BE LEVERAGED BY

Equally important, for protective realism: the doors that are closed.

- **Money.** She has lived close to the bone for decades and the dōjō runs on shoestring funding by choice. Financial pressure produces inconvenience, not leverage.
- **Public shame.** She does not maintain a public profile that shame could damage. Slander reaches her only insofar as it threatens the sword's professional reputation, addressed above.
- **Sexual coercion or romantic entanglement.** Her libido is normative and her intimacy is reserved for tested people. Honeypot operations would be detected quickly and remembered permanently.
- **Pain.** She has a high tolerance and a trained relationship with it. Torture would not extract information she had decided to withhold; it would extract a precise log of who did what, to be addressed later.
- **Threats to her own life.** Operationally inert. She does not negotiate from a position of fearing death; bushidō has done its work here completely.
- **Authority claims.** Badges, titles, ranks, mystical mandates — she evaluates the person, not the credential. The credential is, if anything, a small negative.

---

## XI. SYNTHESIS

The compendium reduces to a single operational sentence: **she is reachable only through the people and frames she has chosen, and breakable only by removing more than one container at once.** Adversaries who understand this will work slowly, indirectly, and on multiple containers in parallel. Allies who understand it will harden the containers preemptively, keep Misty proximate and protected, monitor the inheritance for contamination, prevent a fourth bodily invasion, and decline — under any pressure — to construct dilemmas in which her honor and her chosen kin are forced into competition.

She is the steady one. The protective task is to ensure that what makes her steady is never removed from under her at a moment when she needs it most. The file should be read every six months and updated every time a container changes shape.

*— UATU, observing.*


## Strengths, Assets & Resilience

# UATU DOSSIER — COLLEEN WING
## SECTION VI: STRENGTHS, ASSETS & RESILIENCE
### *The Asset Ledger*

---

## 1. THE PRIMARY WEAPON-SKILL STACK

The asset that has to be named first, because every other asset organizes around it, is her sword work. This is not a generic "martial arts" entry. It is a specific, traceable lineage skill — *Ozawa-derived kenjutsu* with formal *iaidō* (the discipline of drawing-and-cutting from sheath) as its operational signature, supplemented by *battōjutsu* draw-cut variants, *jōdō* (short staff), *tantōjutsu* (knife), and the unarmed grappling auxiliaries that classical Japanese sword schools traditionally bundle (*jūjutsu* fragments, joint-locking, sword-disarm counters). The hours behind it run from roughly age four or five through the present — a continuous training arc of some five decades when accumulated by the publication calendar, and never interrupted for more than days at a time.

The katana itself is the second-tier asset: an *ancestral blade* gifted by Kenji Ozawa, traditionally constructed, properly maintained, and — critically — *the same weapon* across her operational life. Sword fighters bond with a specific weight, balance point, and *kissaki* geometry; the muscle memory is weapon-specific, and continuity of instrument is itself a capability. She knows this blade's harmonic feel through gloves, in rain, in the dark, after a forearm laceration. Replacement would degrade her by a measurable margin for months.

What makes the skill *effective* in a contemporary urban operating environment is the under-appreciated point that *iaidō* is fundamentally a draw-time discipline. The training optimizes the interval between threat-recognition and edge-on-target to fractions of a second from a fully sheathed, non-aggressive starting posture. In a city where weapon display draws law enforcement attention and where pre-deployment of force is socially and legally costly, an operator whose primary skill *begins* from the concealed/sheathed state is uniquely fitted to the terrain. She can stand in a doorway in street clothes, hands visible, and be the first cut in the room.

Auxiliary skill stack: pistol marksmanship at competent-professional rather than elite level (Misty's influence and necessity, not love); knife work in the *tantō* tradition with cross-training in Western fighting-knife; improvised-weapon facility (she can fight with a walking cane, a rolled magazine, a chair leg, the *saya* alone); thrown-blade proficiency; basic explosive familiarity sufficient for breach decisions but not bomb-making.

---

## 2. SOMATIC CAPITAL

A separable asset from skill: the body itself, conditioned over decades into a particular instrument.

Cardiovascular base built on kata repetition rather than running — sustainable rather than peak. She does not sprint well; she lasts. Recovery heart-rate is excellent. **Grip strength** is the single most disproportionate metric — chronic *suburi* (cutting practice with a heavy wooden sword) develops forearm and hand strength to a level most clinicians would call abnormal for her frame. She can hold body weight on a single hand longer than is reasonable. Calloused hands without being mangled; the calluses are placed *correctly* (the heel of the palm, the base of the index finger, the inside of the little finger) — diagnostic to anyone who knows what to look for, including, in a different career, an interrogator.

**Proprioception and balance** are her standout metrics. Decades of kata in low stances develop a postural awareness most people never reach. She knows where her weight is at all times, on any surface. This translates to extraordinary fall-recovery, stair fighting, rooftop work, low-friction floor work, and the ability to *feel* an opponent's weight shift through contact.

**Pain tolerance** is high but, importantly, *informed* rather than dissociative — she does not numb out under pain, she categorizes it (this is muscle, this is tendon, this is bone, this is blood loss, this is shock onset) and triages on the fly. This is the difference between a tough fighter and a survivable one.

**Sleep architecture** is disciplined. She can run on short sleep without degradation longer than most, and she takes restorative micro-sleep (the warrior nap, twelve to twenty minutes, fully unconscious, woken on a self-set internal timer) as a trained skill. She does not require chemical regulation — no caffeine dependence, no sleep aids in the record.

**Hand-eye and reaction time** remain in the upper percentile for her age cohort because the training never stopped. Reflex preserved through use is one of the few capacities that does not meaningfully decline before the seventh decade.

---

## 3. COGNITIVE & PERCEPTUAL ASSETS

**Pattern recognition under threat.** She reads rooms by weight distribution, sightlines, exits, and *posture* — not by faces. This is a different perceptual channel from most operators and gives her information they do not have. She will notice an undrawn weapon by how a man stands on one foot before she notices what his face is doing. In a city full of trained liars whose facial control is excellent and whose postural control is not, this is a substantial edge.

**Tactical patience.** Genuinely exceptional. She can hold a position — physical or rhetorical — for hours without the antsy degradation that compromises most surveillance work. This is partly trained (long *zazen* / seated meditation sessions from childhood) and partly constitutional.

**Decision economy.** Once committed, she does not relitigate. The cost of this is rigidity (covered elsewhere in the file); the benefit is that her commitments are credible and her movements are clean. Allies who plan with her get a known quantity; enemies who try to bait reversal find nothing to grip.

**Multilingual capacity.** Functional Japanese (native-second-language), English (native), reading-level Mandarin and Cantonese (her father's academic environment plus operational necessity in lower-Manhattan/Chinatown work), conversational Korean. Reads classical Japanese well enough to handle period texts — a rare and operationally useful skill in any case involving cultural antiquities, yakuza heritage materials, or Hand-adjacent occult documentation.

**Strategic literacy.** Read in Sun Tzu, Musashi (*Go Rin no Sho*), Yagyū Munenori, Clausewitz at her father's insistence, contemporary counter-insurgency literature absorbed through professional necessity.
